- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** The header search icon's tap target is far below the 44pt iOS minimum: it is a 20pt Icon inside a GestureDetector with no padding/min-size, so the touch area is ~20x20. The '+' button is a 36pt circle (still under 44pt but borderline). The post overflow IconButton is forced to zero with constraints: BoxConstraints() and padding: EdgeInsets.zero, collapsing its hit area to the 20pt glyph.
  - **Fix:** Give the search action a minimum 44x44 hit area (e.g. wrap in a SizedBox(width:44,height:44) or use IconButton with default constraints / a padded GestureDetector). Bump the '+' circle to >=44pt or add surrounding padding. Restore reasonable BoxConstraints on the overflow IconButton once it is functional.
  - **Evidencia:** feed_screen.dart:125 Icon size:20 with no padded target; :131-138 Container 36x36; post_card.dart:106-107 constraints: BoxConstraints(), padding: EdgeInsets.zero.

- **[LOW · design-system]** The 'FEED' title applies typography ad-hoc via GoogleFonts.barlowCondensed(fontSize:28, fontWeight w700, letterSpacing 1.2) instead of a shared text token/theme style. The design system defines headings as Barlow Condensed 700 UPPERCASE letter-spacing 0.5-1.0px; the inline letterSpacing of 1.2 is just outside that range and, more importantly, this heading style is re-declared inline rather than reused. PostCard and FeedSegmentPills also each redeclare similar Barlow Condensed styles inline.
  - **Fix:** Promote section-heading and meta text styles into Theme.of(context).textTheme entries (or an AppText helper) so 'FEED' and similar headers share one definition, and align letterSpacing with the 0.5-1.0 token range. FeedSegmentPills already correctly uses theme.textTheme.labelMedium — extend that pattern to the header and PostCard.
  - **Evidencia:** feed_screen.dart:114-119 inline GoogleFonts.barlowCondensed(letterSpacing:1.2); contrast with feed_segment_pills.dart:79 which uses theme.textTheme.labelMedium.

- **[LOW · responsive]** PostCard body text (post.text, fontSize 14) has no maxLines/overflow guard, which is fine, but the stub stats row ('— kg / — min / — ej.') and the relative-time meta are fixed-size and could crowd at large dynamic-type settings. More notably the empty/error states are vertically centered Columns with mainAxisSize.min and a 48pt icon; with very large accessibility text the message can grow without a scroll fallback, risking clipping on short viewports. The screen was not observed to break, but large-type robustness is untested.
  - **Fix:** When wiring RefreshIndicator (see above), put empty/error content inside a scrollable (SingleChildScrollView + ConstrainedBox/IntrinsicHeight) so large dynamic type can scroll instead of clip. Consider textScaler-aware spacing for the PostCard stats row.
  - **Evidencia:** feed_empty_state.dart:21-37 Center>Column(min) with no scroll; feed_screen.dart:179-194 error Center with fixed padding; post_card.dart:115-122 body Text with no overflow handling.

## lib/features/feed/presentation/create_post_screen.dart (feed module — Create Post / "NUEVO POST")

_Solid on design-system hygiene: every color goes through AppPalette.of(context), the one icon uses TreinoIcon.dumbbell, spacing sticks to the 8/12/14/18/20 scale, and typography uses the Barlow/Barlow Condensed roles correctly. The real gaps are in ACCESSIBILITY and STATES. The header's primary actions (CANCELAR, PUBLICAR) and the privacy pills are bare GestureDetectors with no Semantics, tap targets below 44pt, and the PUBLICAR control becomes an unlabeled spinner while submitting. The over-limit case is a silent dead-end: the counter turns red but PUBLICAR just dims with no explanation. The screen-level loading/error branches are unstyled debug placeholders (Center spinner with no context; raw "Error: $e"). Hardcoded Spanish strings are flagged only as low-severity consistency since the entire feed module follows the same hardcoded pattern (AppL10n is used elsewhere but not in feed)._

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** The header's primary action 'PUBLICAR' is a bare GestureDetector wrapping a Text/spinner with no Semantics button label or button role. While submitting (state.isSubmitting) it renders an 18x18 CircularProgressIndicator with no accessible label at all — a screen reader user hears nothing and cannot tell that the post is being published or that this is the submit control.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the PUBLICAR control in Semantics(button: true, enabled: state.canSubmit, label: 'Publicar') and add a liveRegion/label like 'Publicando…' for the spinner branch. Same treatment for 'CANCELAR' (Semantics(button: true, label: 'Cancelar')). Prefer IconButton/TextButton/InkWell with semantic defaults over GestureDetector for actionable controls.
  - **Evidencia:** _CreatePostHeader, lines 141-152 (CANCELAR GestureDetector) and 166-193 (PUBLICAR GestureDetector + bare CircularProgressIndicator at 177-184)

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** Multiple interactive controls fall below the 44pt minimum tap target. The header text buttons rely on HitTestBehavior.opaque but the hit area is only the glyph height (~14-18px font) — far under 44pt vertically. The privacy pills use padding 18h/8v giving roughly 32-34pt height, also under 44pt. The 18x18 submit spinner replaces the tap target with an 18pt control while submitting.
  - **Fix:** Ensure each tappable area is at least 44x44pt — wrap header actions in a SizedBox/ConstrainedBox(minHeight: 44) or use TextButton with adequate padding, and bump pill vertical padding (or wrap in a 44pt min-height box). Keep the submit control's hit area stable in size between the Text and spinner states.
  - **Evidencia:** Header actions lines 144-152 / 185-192; _PrivacyPill Container padding EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 18, vertical: 8) at line 364; spinner SizedBox(18,18) lines 177-184

- **[HIGH · states]** The screen-level AsyncValue.when loading and error branches are unstyled debug placeholders, not designed states. loading renders a bare Center(CircularProgressIndicator) on the default (likely light Material) background with no AppBackground, no header, no context. error renders Center(Text('Error: \$e')) — raw exception text shown to the user, default red Material style, untokenized, no retry affordance, and a navigational dead-end (no way back to the feed).
  - **Fix:** Wrap both branches in the app's dark background + header (or at least AppBackground) and tokenized typography. Replace the raw 'Error: \$e' with a friendly localized message and a retry/back affordance (ref.invalidate(createPostNotifierProvider) or context.pop()). Reuse FeedEmptyState/equivalent error component already present in the feed module for consistency.
  - **Evidencia:** CreatePostScreen.build, lines 27-31: loading: () => const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()), error: (e, _) => Center(child: Text('Error: \$e'))

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Over-limit input is a silent dead-end. When text exceeds kMaxPostChars (280), the char counter turns danger-red (good) but canSubmit becomes false, so PUBLICAR simply dims to 0.4 opacity with onTap=null and no message. The user gets no explanation of WHY they can't publish — they must infer it from the counter color. This violates visibility of system status and error prevention (Nielsen): the blocked primary action has no stated cause.
  - **Fix:** When charCount > kMaxPostChars, show an inline helper/error near the counter (e.g. 'Te pasaste por N caracteres') so the disabled PUBLICAR has a visible, recognizable cause. Consider also reflecting the over-limit state on the PUBLICAR control via Semantics hint. Optionally enforce maxLength on the TextField if hard truncation is acceptable.
  - **Evidencia:** canSubmit in create_post_notifier.dart lines 35-38 (text.characters.length <= kMaxPostChars); PUBLICAR Opacity(opacity: state.canSubmit ? 1.0 : 0.4, onTap: state.canSubmit ? ... : null) lines 166-174; _CharCounter danger color lines 255-263

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** The char counter ('$charCount / $kMaxPostChars') and the TextField are not linked for screen readers. The TextField has no Semantics label/hint beyond the visual hintText, and the counter is a standalone Text not announced as related to the field, so a screen-reader user editing the post never hears the remaining-character status, including when they cross into the over-limit/danger state.
  - **Fix:** Give the TextField an accessible label (Semantics or InputDecoration with semanticCounterText) and expose the counter as a liveRegion so character count / over-limit is announced as the user types. Color alone (red) is not an accessible signal for the over-limit state.
  - **Evidencia:** _PostTextField lines 218-239 (no semantic label, only hintText); _CharCounter lines 256-264 conveys over-limit via color only

- **[MEDIUM · states]** The 'ETIQUETAR RUTINA' stub chip is permanently disabled (Opacity 0.4, onTap: null) with no indication it is a coming-soon affordance. It looks like a broken/dead control rather than an intentionally future feature, and offers no feedback when a user inevitably taps it. The privacy 'MI GYM' pill is similarly dimmed when !hasGym, but at least has the _PrivacyHelperText nearby; the routine chip has nothing.
  - **Fix:** Either hide the stub until implemented, or mark it as a 'Próximamente' affordance (label/badge) and exclude it from the focus order via Semantics(excludeSemantics or enabled:false). Avoid shipping a control that reads as enabled-but-dead.
  - **Evidencia:** _RoutineTagStubChip lines 412-449: Opacity(opacity: 0.4, GestureDetector(onTap: null, ...))

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** Privacy pills convey selection through color/fill only and are not exposed as a selectable/toggle group to assistive tech. The active pill swaps background to accent and text to bg, but there is no Semantics(selected: true) or radio/segmented-control semantics, so a screen-reader user cannot tell which visibility is chosen or that these are mutually exclusive options. Disabled 'MI GYM' (Opacity 0.4) also has no disabled semantics.
  - **Fix:** Wrap each pill in Semantics(button: true, selected: _isActive, enabled: isEnabled, label: 'Visibilidad: $label') or implement as a proper segmented/radio group. Ensure the disabled pill announces its disabled state and ties to the helper text reason.
  - **Evidencia:** _PrivacyPill lines 359-387 (selection via palette.accent fill only, no Semantics); disabled wrap Opacity(0.4) lines 383-385

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** All user-facing strings are hardcoded Spanish literals (CANCELAR, NUEVO POST, PUBLICAR, VISIBILIDAD, AMIGOS, MI GYM, PÚBLICO, ETIQUETAR RUTINA, '¿Qué querés compartir?', 'Asociate a un gym para postear acá') and the error copy lives in the notifier. The project HAS AppL10n (lib/l10n/app_l10n*.dart) used in auth/coach/reviews modules, but the ENTIRE feed module hardcodes strings — so this screen is consistent with its module, not an outlier. Voseo is correct ('querés', 'Asociate', 'Intentá'). Flagged low because migrating one screen ahead of the module would create inconsistency; it is a module-level debt.
  - **Fix:** Track the feed module's l10n migration as a unit rather than this screen alone. When migrated, move these literals and the notifier's error messages into AppL10n. No screen-local action needed now beyond awareness.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 145, 156, 186, 229, 280, 309/318/327, 398, 436; error strings in create_post_notifier.dart lines 97, 111, 144. Sibling search_users_screen.dart lines 120/157/229 confirm the same hardcoded pattern; rg for AppL10n in lib/features/feed returns nothing.

- **[LOW · visual-hierarchy]** The header title 'NUEVO POST' is visually centered using Spacer() on both sides of a Row whose ends hold variable-width text buttons (CANCELAR vs PUBLICAR/spinner). Because the two side controls differ in width, the title is not truly optically centered and will shift when the PUBLICAR text swaps to the 18pt spinner during submit. Minor, but causes a visible title jump on submit.
  - **Fix:** Use a fixed-width container or a Stack-centered title (or reserve equal min-width for both side actions) so the title stays put and the layout doesn't jump when PUBLICAR becomes a spinner.
  - **Evidencia:** _CreatePostHeader Row with Spacer() at lines 153 and 164 flanking the title; PUBLICAR width changes between Text (185-192) and SizedBox(18,18) spinner (177-184)

## lib/features/feed/presentation/friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart (feed module) — Friend Requests Inbox, incl. child widget widgets/friend_request_inbox_tile.dart

_The screen is clean on the design-system color/typography rules (all colors via AppPalette, Barlow/Barlow Condensed per tokens, spacing on the 8/12/14/18/20 scale) and correctly handles loading/error/empty/data branches of the AsyncValue. The real problems are in accessibility and feedback: tap targets on the back button and action pills are well under 44pt, there are zero Semantics labels on any icon-only control or avatar image (module-wide gap), and accept/reject failures are silently swallowed with no user feedback. There is also a full AppL10n + .arb localization stack in the project that this screen (and the whole feed module) ignores — every user-facing string is hardcoded. Finally, the empty state is bare centered text while the sibling SearchUsersScreen uses the richer FeedEmptyState (icon + text), an in-module inconsistency._

- **[HIGH · states]** Accept (ACEPTAR) and reject (RECHAZAR) actions are fire-and-forget and their catch blocks swallow all errors with empty bodies. If repo.accept/delete throws (offline, permission, Firestore error), the spinner clears, the row stays, and the user gets NO feedback — no snackbar, no inline error, no retry. The user cannot tell whether the action failed or just didn't register. This violates Nielsen's 'visibility of system status' and is the most user-impacting issue on the screen.
  - **Fix:** On catch in _onAceptar/_onRechazar, surface a SnackBar (or inline error) like 'No pudimos aceptar la solicitud. Intentá de nuevo.' so the user knows the action failed and can retry. The dispose-safe ProviderContainer capture is already in place; use a captured ScaffoldMessenger / messenger ref the same way so the message survives the tile's disposal.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_request_inbox_tile.dart _onAceptar lines 164-165 (`catch (_) { // Swallow }`) and _onRechazar lines 184-185 (`catch (_) { // Swallow }`)

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** Action pills RECHAZAR / ACEPTAR have only vertical:8 padding around a 12px line, giving roughly a 30pt-tall hit target — below the 44pt iOS minimum. The two destructive/confirm actions sit 8px apart, increasing mis-tap risk, and ACEPTAR is irreversible (no unfriend/undo from here). Small, closely-spaced, irreversible targets are a real fat-finger hazard.
  - **Fix:** Raise the pill hit area to >=44pt (e.g. wrap in a SizedBox(height: 44) or bump vertical padding) without necessarily enlarging the visual pill, and consider adding a brief undo affordance after ACEPTAR. Keep the 8px visual gap but ensure the actual GestureDetector hit boxes don't overlap.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_request_inbox_tile.dart _InboxActionPill, padding EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal:14, vertical:8) line 222, font size 12 line 234; pills laid out with SizedBox(width:8) between them line 128

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** The back button is a bare Icon (size 20) wrapped in a GestureDetector with HitTestBehavior.opaque but no padding — a ~20pt tap target, far under 44pt — and it has no Semantics label, so a screen reader announces nothing actionable for the only way off this screen. More broadly there are ZERO Semantics labels anywhere in the feed presentation layer: the back icon, the avatar images (PostAvatar), and the icon-only pills are all unlabeled for assistive tech.
  - **Fix:** Give the back control a 44pt hit area (IconButton or a padded GestureDetector) and a Semantics label ('Volver'). Add semanticLabel/Semantics to PostAvatar (e.g. 'Foto de {displayName}') and ensure the pills expose their action label to TalkBack/VoiceOver. This is a module-wide gap worth fixing as a pattern.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart _InboxHeader lines 102-106 (GestureDetector + Icon, no padding, no Semantics); rg shows zero Semantics in lib/features/feed/presentation; PostAvatar (post_avatar.dart) renders images with no semanticLabel

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Every user-facing string is hardcoded in Spanish ('SOLICITUDES', 'No pudimos cargar las solicitudes. Intentá de nuevo.', 'No hay solicitudes pendientes', 'Usuario anónimo', 'RECHAZAR', 'ACEPTAR'). The project ships a complete localization stack — lib/l10n/app_l10n.dart with AppL10n.of(context), intl_es/intl_es_AR/intl_en .arb files, and generate:true in pubspec — and other modules (profile, reviews, check_in) already use AppL10n.of(context).xxx. The entire feed module, including this screen, bypasses it. The voseo itself is correct ('Intentá'), but the strings are not localizable.
  - **Fix:** Move all six strings to .arb keys and read them via AppL10n.of(context) as the rest of the app does (e.g. friendRequestsTitle, friendRequestsLoadError, friendRequestsEmpty, friendRequestAccept, friendRequestReject, profileAnonymousName). Note: localized labels like ACEPTAR/RECHAZAR can be longer in other locales — the pills currently have no maxLines/overflow guard, so verify they don't clip or overflow the row.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart lines 43, 58, 109; friend_request_inbox_tile.dart lines 54, 123, 130; AppL10n.of(context) exists (lib/l10n/app_l10n.dart) and is used in profile_gym_screen.dart etc.; rg -l AppL10n lib/features/feed returns nothing

- **[MEDIUM · consistency]** The empty state here is bare centered text ('No hay solicitudes pendientes'), but the sibling SearchUsersScreen in the same module renders empty/zero-result states through the richer FeedEmptyState widget (a 48px icon + text, centered). Two screens in one module present 'nothing here' two different ways, which reads as unfinished and loses the friendly icon affordance.
  - **Fix:** Reuse FeedEmptyState for the empty branch (e.g. FeedEmptyState(message: ..., icon: TreinoIcon.users or a mail/bell icon)) so the inbox matches search. This also centralizes the empty-state styling.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart data branch lines 53-67 (bare Text); compare search_users_screen.dart lines 229, 257 using FeedEmptyState; widget defined in widgets/feed_empty_state.dart

- **[LOW · consistency]** Mixed icon sourcing for the back control across sibling headers. This screen correctly uses TreinoIcon.back (the design-system-mandated wrapper), but the sibling _SearchUsersHeader uses raw Icons.arrow_back and Icons.close — direct Material icons that bypass TreinoIcon. This screen is the correct one; flagging because the inconsistency makes the module look like it follows two rules.
  - **Fix:** No change needed in friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart (it is already compliant). Worth aligning the sibling search_users_screen.dart to TreinoIcon.back / TreinoIcon.close so the module is uniform.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart line 105 uses TreinoIcon.back (correct); search_users_screen.dart line 116 Icons.arrow_back and line 190 Icons.close (non-compliant siblings)

- **[LOW · states]** The loading state is a bare centered CircularProgressIndicator with no contextual label. For a fast inbox fetch this is acceptable, but a spinner with no text gives no hint of what is loading, especially for screen-reader users (no Semantics) and on slow connections.
  - **Fix:** Optional: add a short label ('Cargando solicitudes...') under the spinner or at minimum a Semantics label so assistive tech announces progress. Low priority given the simple fetch.
  - **Evidencia:** friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart loading branch lines 36-38

## lib/features/feed/presentation/public_profile_screen.dart (feed module — PublicProfileScreen)

_PublicProfileScreen is clean on the design-system color/spacing axis (all colors via AppPalette.of(context), no HEX literals, spacing on the 8/12/14/18/20 scale, all three AsyncValue branches present) — but it diverges sharply from its own sibling, TrainerPublicProfileScreen, on three high-impact axes. (1) NAVIGATION: it renders no Scaffold/AppBar/back button (deliberately, per SCENARIO-207 test) and is pushed as a sub-route under the shell, which only provides a bottom tab bar — so there is NO visible way back; the user is in a dead-end and must use the OS swipe gesture. The sibling Trainer screen wraps in Scaffold+AppBar with a TreinoIcon.back button. (2) I18N: every user-facing string is hardcoded, even though AppL10n (256 keys, used in production) already defines the exact strings — 'No pudimos cargar este perfil.' is literally coachProfileErrorLabel. (3) ACCESSIBILITY: zero Semantics anywhere, the avatar image has no label, the error/loading states give the screen reader nothing, and the tab pills / message stub fall below the 44pt tap-target minimum. The error state is also a dead-end (no retry) where the sibling offers one._

- **[HIGH · navigation]** The screen renders no back affordance. It deliberately omits Scaffold/AppBar/SafeArea (asserted by SCENARIO-207 test, line 88-100) and is pushed as the sub-route /feed/profile/:uid. The shell (_ShellScaffold, router.dart:561) only supplies a bottom tab bar — tapping a tab calls context.go() and replaces the stack, it does not pop. So a user who taps into a public profile has NO on-screen way back: there is no AppBar back arrow, no close button, and the bottom bar does not pop. They depend entirely on the iOS edge-swipe gesture (which the branch name fix/workout-swipe-back suggests is itself fragile). This is a navigational dead-end and directly contradicts the sibling TrainerPublicProfileScreen, which wraps in Scaffold + AppBar + an IconButton(TreinoIcon.back) leading widget (trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:30-40).
  - **Fix:** Mirror TrainerPublicProfileScreen: wrap the body in a Scaffold (transparent background, so it still composites over the shell's AppBackground) with a transparent AppBar whose leading is IconButton(icon: Icon(TreinoIcon.back), onPressed: () => context.canPop() ? context.pop() : context.go('/feed')). If the no-Scaffold composition is a hard requirement, at minimum add a back/close TreinoIcon button overlaid on the hero. Update SCENARIO-207 accordingly.
  - **Evidencia:** public_profile_screen.dart:40 (SingleChildScrollView is the root, no Scaffold/AppBar); test SCENARIO-207 (public_profile_screen_test.dart:88-100) asserts no Scaffold; router.dart:363-369 (pushed sub-route) vs sibling trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:30-40 (has AppBar + back).

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Every user-facing string is hardcoded in Spanish literals, violating design-system rule #3 ('Nunca hard-code de strings de UI'). Worse, the AppL10n layer already exists, is used in production (e.g. trainer_public_profile_screen.dart imports and uses it heavily), has 256 keys, and already defines the EXACT strings this screen reinvents: the hardcoded 'No pudimos cargar este perfil.' (line 96) is byte-for-byte identical to AppL10n.coachProfileErrorLabel (app_l10n_es.dart:188). The screen also hardcodes 'MENSAJE' (129), 'RUTINAS PÚBLICAS' (156), 'ACTIVIDAD' (167), 'Aún no hay rutinas públicas.' (232), 'Aún no hay actividad reciente.' (233), plus stat labels in the child row ('WORKOUTS', 'RACHA', 'SEGUIDORES', 'SIGUIENDO' — public_profile_stats_row.dart:34-54) and the follow-button labels ('SEGUIR', 'SIGUIENDO', 'SOLICITUD ENVIADA', 'ACEPTAR' — public_profile_follow_button.dart). The CLAUDE.md note 'cuando llegue Fase 6' is stale — Fase 6 has arrived (lib/l10n/ is populated and live).
  - **Fix:** Route all strings through AppL10n.of(context). Reuse coachProfileErrorLabel for the error fallback; add feed-scoped keys (e.g. feedProfileTabRoutines, feedProfileTabActivity, feedProfileRoutinesEmpty, feedProfileActivityEmpty, feedProfileMessageCta) in app_l10n_es.dart / _en.dart. This also unblocks the EN locale, which is currently completely missing for this screen.
  - **Evidencia:** public_profile_screen.dart:96,129,156,167,232,233; identical key already at app_l10n_es.dart:188 (coachProfileErrorLabel); design-system.md rule #3 (line 95).

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** No Semantics anywhere in the screen or any of its child widgets (grep for Semantics/semanticLabel/excludeSemantics returns zero hits across all 5 files). Concrete failures: (a) the avatar (PostAvatar, 96px hero image, post_avatar.dart) exposes no label — a screen reader announces nothing or a raw URL; it should carry the person's name. (b) The icon-bearing follow button is fine (it has a text label) but the disabled MENSAJE stub uses GestureDetector(onTap: null) wrapped only in Opacity 0.6 — VoiceOver gets no 'disabled' / 'button' semantics, just static text. (c) The loading state is a bare CircularProgressIndicator with no Semantics label, so a screen reader announces nothing while data loads (fails Nielsen 'visibility of system status' for AT users). (d) The error state Text is not flagged as an alert/liveRegion.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the avatar+name block in Semantics(label: view.authorDisplayName, image/header: true) or pass a semanticLabel into PostAvatar. Give the MENSAJE stub Semantics(button: true, enabled: false, label: 'Mensaje (próximamente)'). Add Semantics(label: l10n loading) around the spinner or use a SemanticsService announcement. Mark the error text liveRegion: true.
  - **Evidencia:** Zero Semantics hits across public_profile_screen.dart, public_profile_hero.dart, public_profile_stats_row.dart, public_profile_follow_button.dart, post_avatar.dart; spinner at public_profile_screen.dart:89-91; MENSAJE stub at lines 109-141.

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** Tap targets fall below the 44pt iOS minimum. The tab pills (_ProfilePill) use vertical padding of only 8px with a 12px font (public_profile_screen.dart:196) → roughly 30-32pt tall. The MENSAJE stub and follow pill use vertical:12 → ~37-40pt, still under 44. These are GestureDetector with HitTestBehavior.opaque, so the hit area equals the visible box; there is no expanded touch slop. Small toggle pills are exactly the controls that need the full 44pt.
  - **Fix:** Raise the pill hit area to >=44pt: either bump vertical padding (e.g. to a 12-14 token to reach ~44pt) or wrap each GestureDetector in a SizedBox(height: 44)/ConstrainedBox(minHeight: 44). Keeping the visual pill small while enlarging the hit region is acceptable.
  - **Evidencia:** public_profile_screen.dart:196 (_ProfilePill padding vertical:8), lines 121 & 178 (vertical:12 for message/follow pills).

- **[MEDIUM · states]** The error branch is a passive dead-end: it shows only static text 'No pudimos cargar este perfil.' with no retry action (public_profile_screen.dart:92-104). The user cannot recover without leaving the screen — and as noted above there is also no back button, compounding the trap. The sibling TrainerPublicProfileScreen's error state offers a retry button that invalidates the provider (trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:45-46, 133-160). Additionally, data success has no distinct empty-vs-populated treatment for the profile itself (tabs always show placeholder copy because content is wired in a later phase — acceptable for now, but the error path is a real regression vs the sibling).
  - **Fix:** Add a retry affordance to the error state: a TextButton/ghost button that calls ref.invalidate(publicProfileViewProvider(targetUid)), matching the sibling's pattern and Nielsen 'user control & freedom'. Reuse AppL10n.coachRetryLabel.
  - **Evidencia:** public_profile_screen.dart:92-104 (error = text only); sibling retry at trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:45-46 and _ErrorState 133-160.

- **[MEDIUM · consistency]** Two profile screens for conceptually the same surface (athlete public profile vs trainer public profile, same feed/coach pattern) are structurally inconsistent. Trainer: Scaffold+AppBar+back, ListView with bottom MediaQuery inset, AppL10n strings, named _ErrorState/_NotFoundState/retry, body text via TextStyle. Athlete (this screen): no chrome, SingleChildScrollView, hardcoded strings, inline error, GoogleFonts.barlow inline. This divergence makes the two flows feel like different apps and doubles maintenance. Also note this screen uses GoogleFonts.* directly inline for every text style rather than any shared text-style tokens — consistent with the rest of the codebase so not a defect per se, but it amplifies drift between the two screens.
  - **Fix:** Align this screen's shell (Scaffold/AppBar/back), error handling (retry), and string source (AppL10n) with TrainerPublicProfileScreen so both public-profile surfaces share one mental model. Consider extracting a shared profile scaffold if a third profile screen is likely.
  - **Evidencia:** Compare public_profile_screen.dart (whole file) against trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:30-101.

## lib/features/feed/presentation/search_users_screen.dart (feed module — full-screen user search)

_Solid, well-structured screen: a complete state machine (initial / below-min / loading / empty-results / error / data), correct AppPalette token usage for all colors (zero HEX literals), debounce in the widget keeping the provider pure, and a header/list/empty-state pattern consistent with its closest sibling (FriendRequestsInboxScreen). The real issues are concentrated in two areas. (1) Icons: this is the ONLY file in the entire feed module that uses raw Material `Icons.*` (arrow_back, close) instead of the mandated `TreinoIcon.X` wrapper — and exact equivalents (TreinoIcon.back, TreinoIcon.close) already exist, so it's a clear, avoidable design-system violation. (2) Accessibility: icon-only tap targets (back button, clear button) are bare 18–20pt Icons inside GestureDetectors with no 44pt hit box and no Semantics labels; the search field also lacks input affordances (textInputAction, autocorrect off). Hardcoded Spanish strings are real but are a module-wide condition (0/14 feed files use AppL10n, while the coach module uses it consistently) — flagged at lower severity as a consistency gap rather than a screen-specific defect. No invented problems; the screen is genuinely above average for the codebase._

- **[HIGH · design-system]** This screen uses raw Material icons (Icons.arrow_back in the header, Icons.close as the clear-field suffix) instead of the mandated TreinoIcon.X wrapper. AGENTS.md / design-system.md rule #2 is explicit: 'Nunca PhosphorIcons/Material icons directo — usar TreinoIcon.X'. This is the ONLY file in the entire feed module that breaks the rule — every sibling (FriendRequestsInboxScreen, etc.) uses TreinoIcon.back. The wrapper exists for exactly this purpose (single source of truth for icon family swaps), and the needed constants already exist (TreinoIcon.back, TreinoIcon.close).
  - **Fix:** Replace Icons.arrow_back (line 116) with TreinoIcon.back and Icons.close (line 190) with TreinoIcon.close. No new icon constants are required — both already exist in lib/core/widgets/treino_icon.dart (lines 31 and 33). Note: TreinoIcon.back is caretLeft, which is the same back glyph all sibling feed headers render, so this also fixes a subtle visual inconsistency (this screen currently shows an arrow, siblings show a caret).
  - **Evidencia:** search_users_screen.dart:116 (Icon(Icons.arrow_back ...)) and :190 (Icon(Icons.close ...)); contrast with friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart:105 (Icon(TreinoIcon.back ...)); treino_icon.dart:31,33 confirm TreinoIcon.back/close exist.

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** Both icon-only controls fail the 44pt minimum tap target and have no screen-reader label. The header back button is an Icon(size: 20) inside a GestureDetector with no padding/constraints (~20pt hit box). The clear-field button is an Icon(size: 18) inside a GestureDetector (~18pt). Neither is wrapped in Semantics, so VoiceOver announces them as unlabeled/generic. iOS HIG and WCAG 2.5.5 require >=44pt; an 18–20pt target is roughly a third of that and is a real miss-tap risk, especially the clear button which sits at the field edge.
  - **Fix:** Wrap each GestureDetector target so its hit area is >=44x44 (e.g. SizedBox(width: 44, height: 44) with the icon centered, or use IconButton with default constraints) and add Semantics labels: back button -> Semantics(button: true, label: 'Volver'); clear button -> Semantics(button: true, label: 'Limpiar búsqueda'). For the clear button consider IconButton which gives both the tap target and tooltip/semantics for free. Note: no Semantics appears anywhere in feed or coach modules, so this is a codebase-wide gap, but a search screen is a high-traffic place to start fixing it.
  - **Evidencia:** search_users_screen.dart:113-117 (back GestureDetector, Icon size 20, no constraints); :188-191 (clear GestureDetector, Icon size 18); grep confirms zero Semantics/semanticLabel in this screen, its tile, and the empty state.

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** The TextField has no input configuration tuned for a name-search use case. There is no textInputAction (keyboard shows a generic newline/return rather than a 'Search'/'Buscar' action), autocorrect and autocapitalization are left at defaults (autocorrect on + sentence capitalization will fight a username/handle search and inject unwanted corrections), and there is no autofocus, so the user lands on a search screen and must take an extra tap to start typing.
  - **Fix:** Set textInputAction: TextInputAction.search, autocorrect: false, textCapitalization: TextCapitalization.none (or .words if matching display names), and consider autofocus: true so the keyboard opens on entry. Optionally hook onSubmitted to flush the debounce immediately. These directly improve 'recognition over recall' and reduce friction on a screen whose sole purpose is typing a query.
  - **Evidencia:** search_users_screen.dart:153-201 (_SearchTextField) — no textInputAction, keyboardType, autocorrect, textCapitalization, or autofocus set.

- **[MEDIUM · states]** The empty-results and error states are handled (good), but two state-quality gaps remain. (1) The loading spinner (CircularProgressIndicator at line 239) has no accompanying context/label — a bare spinner on a screen that also shows an identical-looking centered layout for empty states; VoiceOver users get no 'Buscando…' status (violates Nielsen 'visibility of system status'). (2) The 'typing-below-min' branch (1 char typed) silently reuses the exact initial prompt 'Buscá usuarios por nombre', so a user who typed one letter gets zero feedback that a 2-char minimum exists — it looks like nothing happened.
  - **Fix:** (1) Pair the spinner with a muted 'Buscando…' label and/or a Semantics(liveRegion: true) wrapper so the search status is announced. (2) For 0 < len < kSearchMinChars, show a distinct hint such as 'Escribí al menos 2 caracteres' instead of the generic initial prompt, so the minimum-length gate is discoverable.
  - **Evidencia:** search_users_screen.dart:232-234 (below-min branch returns same FeedEmptyState message as the initial branch at :229); :238-241 (loading -> bare CircularProgressIndicator, no label/semantics).

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** All user-facing strings are hardcoded Spanish literals ('BUSCAR USUARIOS', 'Buscar por nombre', 'Buscá usuarios por nombre', 'Sin resultados para "..."', the error copy) despite the project shipping a full AppL10n system (lib/l10n with intl_es / intl_es_AR / intl_en arb files). The coach module uses AppL10n.of(context) consistently; the feed module does not (0 of 14 feed presentation files import app_l10n). So this is a module-wide debt, not unique to this screen — hence low severity here — but it is still a real design-system rule violation (rule #3: 'Nunca hard-code de strings de UI'). Voseo is correct ('Buscá'). Minor truncation risk: 'Sin resultados para "$activeQuery"' has no maxLines/overflow and could wrap awkwardly for a long pasted query, and the 'BUSCAR USUARIOS' header has no overflow guard for longer localized variants.
  - **Fix:** When the feed module is localized (ideally as one batch to keep it consistent with coach), move these literals to AppL10n keys: feedSearchTitle, feedSearchHint, feedSearchInitialPrompt, feedSearchBelowMinHint, feedSearchNoResults (parameterized with the query), feedSearchError. Until then, at minimum add maxLines/overflow to the no-results message and the header Text so longer strings degrade gracefully.
  - **Evidencia:** search_users_screen.dart:120,157,229,233,246,258 (hardcoded strings); grep: 0 feed presentation files import app_l10n vs coach using AppL10n.of(context) (athlete_agenda_screen.dart:48,125,178); lib/l10n/intl_es_AR.arb exists.

## lib/features/home/home_screen.dart (home module: HomeScreen, _AthleteHome, HomeHeader, EmpezarEntrenamientoCard, EstaSemanaCard, HomeCTAButton, BodySilhouettePlaceholder; sibling TrainerDashboardTab)

_Home screen is strong on the design-system axis: no HEX literals, no direct PhosphorIcons (all icons via TreinoIcon), palette tokens via AppPalette.of(context), and the documented spacing scale is respected. State coverage is good - EstaSemanaCard is exemplary, with distinct skeleton, error fallback, motivating empty state, and loaded state via AsyncValue.when. The dominant issue is i18n: the athlete home (HomeHeader, EmpezarEntrenamientoCard, EstaSemanaCard) hardcodes every user-facing string, while its sibling TrainerDashboardTab - rendered by the same HomeScreen role split - already uses AppL10n.of(context) against an existing voseo intl_es_AR.arb, so one screen mixes localized and non-localized text. Secondary issues: zero Semantics anywhere in the module (avatar and decorative icons unlabeled), fixed-size hero texts that risk clipping under large dynamic type, an undiscoverable whole-card tap on EstaSemanaCard, inconsistent go vs push navigation, and the placeholder EmpezarEntrenamientoCard that will need real async states once wired. Voseo Spanish in existing copy is correct (entrena hoy, no rompas la racha, hace el primero).</parameter>
</invoke>
_

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Every user-facing string in the athlete home is hardcoded, despite a working AppL10n infrastructure that the sibling widget in the same screen already uses. HomeScreen renders either TrainerDashboardTab (which calls AppL10n.of(context) for section labels and stat captions) or the athlete home (which hardcodes everything), so one screen mixes localized and non-localized text. Hardcoded strings include the greeting HOLA / HOLA NAME in home_header.dart, the entire EmpezarEntrenamientoCard (HOY JUEVES, PUSH, the muscle subtitle, 6 ejercicios, 55 min, EMPEZAR ENTRENAMIENTO), and all of EstaSemanaCard (ESTA SEMANA, RACHA ACTUAL, PRIMER PASO, DIAS, the empty title, EXPLORAR RUTINAS, the insights error body, the streak subtext lines, SEMANA/MES/entrenos, and the _monthsEs abbreviations). design-system.md rule 3 forbids hardcoded UI strings.
  - **Fix:** Move every athlete-home string into intl_es_AR.arb with home keys (homeGreeting with a name placeholder, homeEmpezarHeroLabel, homeEstaSemanaTitle, homeRachaActualPill, homeEmptyTitle, homeEmptyCta, homeInsightsErrorBody, homeStreakSubtextTrained/Untrained, etc.) and read them via AppL10n.of(context), exactly as TrainerDashboardTab already does. Move _monthsEs and _dayLabels to intl or DateFormat so dates localize too.
  - **Evidencia:** home_header.dart lines 28-30; empezar_entrenamiento_card.dart lines 15-20; esta_semana_card.dart lines 91, 123, 133, 187, 261-262, 282, 302-303, 328-341, 374, 544, 565; contrast trainer_dashboard_tab.dart lines 59, 67, 382, 395 which use AppL10n. grep confirms 0 AppL10n references in lib/features/home/.

- **[HIGH · accessibility]** The module contains zero Semantics widgets (confirmed by grep across lib/features/home/ and trainer_dashboard_tab.dart). Most critically the user avatar in HomeHeader (CachedNetworkImage plus gradient fallback) has no semantic label, so screen readers announce nothing for the most prominent identity element. Standalone decorative icons (the streak flame in the empty state, the colored status dot in the RACHA ACTUAL pill) are also unlabeled, and the bell-with-badge in the trainer header conveys a pending-requests count purely visually.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the avatar in a Semantics node with an image label (foto de perfil de NAME, or Perfil when null). Mark purely decorative icons (flame, status dot, body silhouettes) with ExcludeSemantics so VoiceOver skips them, and give the bell-with-badge a Semantics label like N solicitudes pendientes. All labels through AppL10n.
  - **Evidencia:** home_header.dart lines 34-53 (avatar, no Semantics); esta_semana_card.dart line 274 (flame), lines 364-371 (status dot); trainer_dashboard_tab.dart lines 148-183 (bell badge); grep shows no Semantics anywhere in the module.

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** Several hero texts use large fixed font sizes inside height-constrained or single-line layouts, creating clipping/overflow risk under large dynamic type. The worst is the streak number Text with fontSize 96 and height 1, sitting in a Row (crossAxisAlignment end) next to a fixed-padding DIAS label; with textScaler above 1 and a two-digit streak this can overflow horizontally. PUSH (fontSize 36) and the greeting (fontSize 28) have no maxLines or overflow handling, and the empty-state title uses a hardcoded two-line break that re-wraps badly when scaled.
  - **Fix:** Wrap large numeric and hero text in FittedBox(fit: BoxFit.scaleDown) or set maxLines plus TextOverflow, and use baseline alignment for the streak/DIAS row so it survives scaling. Test at MediaQuery textScaler 1.3 to 2.0 and avoid hardcoded line breaks.
  - **Evidencia:** esta_semana_card.dart lines 174-181 (streak 96), 261-270 (empty title), 266 and 558 (32); empezar_entrenamiento_card.dart lines 49-57 (PUSH 36); home_header.dart lines 60-68 (greeting 28, Expanded but no maxLines).

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** EstaSemanaCard is fully tappable (GestureDetector onTap navigating to /home/insights with HitTestBehavior.opaque) but offers no visual affordance that it is interactive: no chevron, no ver mas label, no ripple. The card also contains its own CTAs and tap targets, so the whole-card tap is both undiscoverable and ambiguous, because tapping the embedded EXPLORAR RUTINAS button versus the surrounding card goes to different routes. Sibling TrainerDashboardTab rows use InkWell (ripple) and explicit trailing carets.
  - **Fix:** Add an explicit affordance: a trailing caret or VER INSIGHTS label in the card header, or convert the whole-card tap to InkWell for a ripple. Ensure the empty-state CTA and the card tap do not silently compete; ideally the empty state should not also be wrapped in a navigating gesture.
  - **Evidencia:** esta_semana_card.dart lines 58-74 (GestureDetector opaque, no affordance) versus trainer_dashboard_tab.dart lines 623 and 757 (InkWell) and line 524 (explicit forward caret).

- **[LOW · navigation]** Navigation method is inconsistent for similarly presented destinations. The two go-to-workout actions use context.go(/workout), which replaces the stack, while the insights link uses context.push(/home/insights) which stacks and yields a back affordance. If /workout is a shell tab switch then go is correct, but mixing go and push for similar in-app cards risks an inconsistent back-button experience.
  - **Fix:** Define intent per route: context.go only for bottom-bar tab switches and context.push for detail or sub-screens, applied uniformly, and document the convention. Verify the back behavior after each CTA matches user expectation.
  - **Evidencia:** esta_semana_card.dart line 59 (push) versus line 293 (go); empezar_entrenamiento_card.dart line 99 (go); home_screen.dart line 116 (push for resume).

- **[LOW · states]** The top-level athlete home intentionally renders the athlete view while role is loading (a documented tradeoff) and HomeHeader shows a 56px skeleton while the profile loads, both reasonable. However EmpezarEntrenamientoCard is entirely hardcoded placeholder data with no async branch of its own; once wired to a real today-routine provider it will need loading, empty (no routine or rest day), and error states. As-is it always shows the same fake Thursday PUSH session regardless of the real day or assignment, a visibility-of-system-status gap the moment real data exists.
  - **Fix:** When wiring the card to a routine provider, add the three async branches (skeleton, empty or rest-day, error) mirroring EstaSemanaCard. Until then avoid a hardcoded weekday that can contradict the real date shown elsewhere.
  - **Evidencia:** empezar_entrenamiento_card.dart lines 9-21 (static const placeholder, no AsyncValue handling); compare EstaSemanaCard loading/error/empty/loaded at esta_semana_card.dart lines 67-73.

## lib/features/insights/presentation/insights_screen.dart (module: insights)

_Solid, on-brand screen: zero HEX literals, all colors via AppPalette, all icons via TreinoIcon, all four AsyncValue states (loading/error/empty/data) present, and a thoughtfully handled "no routine assigned" sub-state in the volume card. Two real, high-value issues stand out against sibling screens in the same app: (1) every user-facing string is hardcoded Spanish while 50 other files localize via AppL10n — a direct violation of design-system rule #3 and a consistency break; (2) the error state discards the error and offers no retry, making it a dead-end, unlike sibling sections (historial/mi_plan) that ship a retry CTA. Accessibility has gaps (back button and body image lack semantic labels). The rest is polish-level._

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Every user-facing string on the screen is a hardcoded Spanish literal: header 'INSIGHTS' (L88), error 'No pudimos cargar tus insights.' (L37), empty 'Empezá a entrenar para ver tus insights.' (L131), volume hint 'Necesitás una rutina asignada...' (L446), card titles 'MÚSCULOS DE LA SEMANA' (L323) / 'VOLUMEN POR GRUPO' (L435), 'SETS' (L401), '$done / $target sets' (L502), 'SEMANA · ...' range + month abbreviations (L559-567), and the 'VOLVER' button (L544). Design-system rule #3 explicitly forbids hardcoded UI strings, and 50 other files across workout/coach/profile already route every string through AppL10n.of(context). This screen is the outlier.
  - **Fix:** Move all strings to the ARB files (intl_es_AR.arb for voseo, plus en) and read them via AppL10n.of(context), matching sibling screens like historial_section.dart and mi_plan_section.dart. Use an ICU plural for the 'sets' suffix and a DateFormat (intl) for the week range / month names instead of the hand-rolled _monthsEs array so localization and formatting stay consistent.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L37, L88, L131, L323, L401, L435, L446, L502, L544, L559-567

- **[HIGH · states]** The error branch ignores the error object (`error: (_, __)`) and renders only a static caption with no recovery affordance (L33-45). The user cannot retry without leaving the screen — a dead-end. Sibling AsyncValue handlers in the same app pair the error message with an explicit retry/CTA button: historial_section.dart (_ListErrorState with onRetry, workoutHistorialErrorRetry) and mi_plan_section.dart (_SectionErrorState).
  - **Fix:** Add a 'Reintentar' TextButton/OutlinedButton under the error message that calls `ref.invalidate(weeklyInsightsProvider)` (or ref.refresh), mirroring _ListErrorState in historial_section.dart. This restores user control & freedom (Nielsen) and aligns with the module's established error pattern.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L33-45; cf. historial_section.dart _ListErrorState, mi_plan_section.dart _SectionErrorState

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** The back IconButton (L82-85) has no tooltip and no Semantics label, so a screen reader announces it only as an unlabeled button. The decorative back arrow gives no spoken affordance. (Note: athlete_detail_screen.dart sets tooltip on its icon buttons, so labeled icon buttons are an established norm in the project.)
  - **Fix:** Add `tooltip: AppL10n.of(context).commonBack` (or wrap in Semantics(button: true, label: ...)). This also surfaces a hover/long-press label and a TalkBack/VoiceOver hint.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L82-85

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** The body silhouette Image.asset widgets in BodySilhouettePlaceholder (_BodyImage, body_silhouette_placeholder.dart L106-117) have no semanticLabel and are not excluded from the semantics tree. A screen reader either skips them silently or, worse, the surrounding 'MÚSCULOS DE LA SEMANA' card reads as a bare image with no description of what it represents.
  - **Fix:** Either add a semanticLabel describing the figure (e.g. 'Silueta corporal de grupos musculares') via Semantics(image: true, label: ...), or wrap purely-decorative instances in ExcludeSemantics so the muscle list (which carries the real data) is the screen-reader source of truth.
  - **Evidencia:** body_silhouette_placeholder.dart L106-117

- **[MEDIUM · responsive]** Font sizes are fixed px (GoogleFonts) and several containers have fixed dimensions: BodySilhouettePlaceholder width:160/height:240 (L335) and _DayChip 36x36 circles (L249-299). With large OS dynamic type, _MuscleSetsRow (L372-409: dot + Expanded label + fixed 16px count + 'SETS') and the day-chip numbers risk clipping/overflow, and the 240px silhouette won't grow with text. The week-strip row of 7 chips can also crowd on narrow devices at large scale.
  - **Fix:** Test at MediaQuery textScaler ~1.5x. Consider FittedBox/Flexible around the day-of-month text inside chips and the trailing count in _MuscleSetsRow, and allow the muscle label to wrap or ellipsize. If localized labels (e.g. longer than 'PIERNAS') push the row, add maxLines/overflow handling.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L335, L249-299, L372-409

- **[LOW · design-system]** Spacing mostly respects the 8/12/14/18/20 scale, but _MusclesCard uses `EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 4)` (L343), and the design-system doc explicitly says NOT to use 4. There are also bare typographic literals (fontSize: 11 L404, 13 L385/L449/L495; letterSpacing 0.8) that aren't drawn from any shared typography token — acceptable today since the app has no TextStyle token system yet, but they drift from the documented scale.
  - **Fix:** Bump the vertical: 4 row padding to the nearest scale value (8) or absorb it via a SizedBox(height: 8) between rows. Longer term, extract the repeated Barlow Condensed 12px/700/ls1.2 muted 'section eyebrow' style (used identically at L174, L322, L434) into a shared TextStyle helper to kill the duplication.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L343; repeated eyebrow style L174/L322/L434

- **[LOW · states]** The loading state is a bare centered CircularProgressIndicator with no contextual label (L30-32). Per Nielsen 'visibility of system status', a spinner alone gives no indication of what is loading.
  - **Fix:** Optional polish: add a short caption (e.g. 'Calculando tu semana…' via AppL10n) below the spinner, consistent with the eliminarCuentaSheet loading pattern which pairs a spinner with a label/subtitle.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L30-32

- **[LOW · navigation]** The screen offers two redundant back affordances — the header back IconButton (L82) and the full-width 'VOLVER' button at the bottom of the list (L528-555) — both calling the same _safePopOrHome. This is harmless and arguably good for reachability, but the bottom button competes visually with what should be the screen's primary action; an Insights screen has no obvious primary CTA, so a prominent pill-shaped 'VOLVER' reads like the main action when it is really secondary navigation.
  - **Fix:** Keep it (mockup-driven) but consider styling 'VOLVER' as a ghost/text button rather than a full pill OutlinedButton so it doesn't read as the primary CTA, or drop it and rely on the header back since this screen is push-navigated and always has a back target.
  - **Evidencia:** insights_screen.dart L82-85 and L528-555

## lib/features/measurements/presentation/log_measurement_screen.dart (measurements module)

_The screen is visually on-brand and disciplined about design tokens: every color goes through AppPalette.of(context), the only icon (chevron) uses TreinoIcon, radii/spacing largely follow the token scale, and typography uses the Barlow/Barlow Condensed conventions consistently with its sibling chart widget. The save flow handles loading and success/error via SnackBars. The two material problems are: (1) it is the single biggest i18n regression in the module — every user-facing string is hardcoded in Spanish while the parent athlete_detail_screen.dart and ~50 other files use AppL10n.of(context); and (2) accessibility/usability gaps around the form: no field validation or error prevention (silently drops un-parseable numbers, allows saving a completely empty measurement), the collapsed CIRCUMFERENCES section gives no signal that data was entered inside it, and there is no Semantics/labelling guarantee for the chevron-only expander. Several smaller spacing-token and tap-target issues round it out._

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Every user-facing string in this screen is hardcoded Spanish literal. Examples: 'Cancelar' (line 248), 'Cargar medición' (261), 'COMPOSICIÓN CORPORAL' (289), 'Peso (kg)' / 'Grasa (%)' / 'Masa muscular (kg)' (292-305), 'NOTAS' (334), 'Observaciones del entrenador…' (347), 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN' (385), 'CIRCUNFERENCIAS' (628), 'Opcional. Cargá las que quieras.' (638), section labels 'TRONCO/TREN SUPERIOR/TREN INFERIOR' (665/702/725), every field label (Hombros, Pecho, Cintura...), the bilateral hints 'I (cm)'/'D (cm)' (527/542), and all three SnackBar messages (168, 210, 218). The immediate parent (athlete_detail_screen.dart) and ~50 other files use AppL10n.of(context). This screen is a complete i18n regression inside an otherwise-localized module.
  - **Fix:** Move all strings to lib/l10n/app_l10n_*.dart and read them via AppL10n.of(context), matching the parent screen. The voseo present ('Cargá las que quieras', 'Probá de nuevo') is correct Rioplatense — preserve that tone in the es-AR ARB.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 168, 210, 218, 248, 261, 289, 292-305, 334, 347, 385, 527, 542, 628, 638, 665, 668-746

- **[HIGH · usability]** No error prevention or input validation. _parseDouble (153-157) returns null for any unparseable string and the value is silently dropped — a trainer typing '7o' or '12.3.4' loses that metric with zero feedback, and the success SnackBar still says 'Medición guardada'. There are no min/max sanity bounds (negative or absurd values save fine). Worse, an entirely empty form saves a Measurement where every field is null (the only guard is trainerUid != null at 231/365), creating a meaningless record. This violates Nielsen #5 (error prevention) and #1 (visibility of system status — the user thinks data was saved that wasn't).
  - **Fix:** Add inputFormatters (FilteringTextInputFormatter for decimals) to reject invalid characters at entry, validate ranges, and disable GUARDAR or show an inline error when zero metrics are present. Surface per-field invalid input instead of silently nulling it. A Form + GlobalKey<FormState> with validators is the idiomatic fit here.
  - **Evidencia:** _parseDouble lines 153-157; _save guard line 162-173; canSave line 231; no Form/validator anywhere

- **[MEDIUM · states]** The collapsible CIRCUMFERENCES section gives no indication when it contains entered data once collapsed. A trainer can fill several circumferences, collapse the panel, and the header looks identical to an empty panel — easy to forget filled data exists or to assume it was cleared. The subtitle stays the static 'Opcional. Cargá las que quieras.' regardless of state. This is a recognition-over-recall gap (Nielsen #6).
  - **Fix:** When collapsed and any inner controller is non-empty, show a filled-count badge or change the subtitle (e.g. 'N cargadas') and/or tint the chevron with palette.accent so the user recognizes there is data inside without expanding.
  - **Evidencia:** _CircumferencesSection header lines 627-651; subtitle line 638; collapsed branch gated by _expanded line 658

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** The CIRCUMFERENCES expand/collapse control is a chevron-only affordance with no Semantics. The InkWell (616) wraps a header whose only state indicator for screen readers is the visual chevron icon (647-651), which carries no semantic label and no expanded/collapsed announcement. VoiceOver users get no 'expanded'/'collapsed' state. Additionally the chevron Icon size is 16 with no enlarged hit area beyond the row padding, though the full-width InkWell mitigates the tap target here.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the header in Semantics(button: true, expanded: _expanded, label: <localized 'Circunferencias'>) or use an ExpansionTile which provides this for free. Mark the decorative chevron excludeSemantics.
  - **Evidencia:** InkWell line 616; chevron Icon lines 647-651; no Semantics widget in file

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** Large dynamic type / clipping risk in the top bar. The title block (257-276) is a right-aligned Column inside a Row next to a 'Cancelar' TextButton with a Spacer; the title 'Cargar medición' and date use fixed fontSize 16/12 with no maxLines/overflow handling. Under large text scale or a longer localized title, the Column has no width constraint and can overflow the Row against the Cancelar button. Fixed font sizes throughout (12-16) ignore the user's text-scale preference and the bilateral hints 'I (cm)'/'D (cm)' in narrow half-width fields are tight.
  - **Fix:** Constrain/Flexible the title Column and add maxLines + TextOverflow.ellipsis; verify the screen at textScaleFactor 1.3-2.0. Prefer Theme text styles that respect scaling over hardcoded fontSize where feasible.
  - **Evidencia:** Top bar Row lines 242-277; title Text lines 260-274; no maxLines/Flexible; bilateral hints lines 527/542

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** No unsaved-changes guard (Nielsen #3 user control & freedom, but inverted — too easy to lose work). Tapping 'Cancelar' (245) or the iOS back/swipe on this fullscreenDialog pops immediately and discards all entered metrics with no confirmation. Given the form can hold ~20 manually measured values, an accidental dismissal is costly.
  - **Fix:** Add a PopScope/WillPopScope that, when any controller is dirty, prompts a confirm-discard dialog before popping (and route the Cancelar button through the same check).
  - **Evidencia:** Cancelar onPressed line 245-246; no PopScope/WillPopScope in build (234-399)

- **[LOW · design-system]** Off-scale spacing values. The design system restricts spacing to 8·12·14·18·20 and explicitly forbids 4/16/24. This screen uses SizedBox(height: 6) at lines 475 and 512 (label-to-field gap), SizedBox(width: 8)/height values that are fine, but also SizedBox(height: 2) at line 636 and SizedBox(width: 4) is avoided — the 6 and 2 values are off the allowed scale. Top bar padding fromLTRB(8,8,20,0) mixes scale values acceptably, but the 6px gaps recur via the shared _numericField/_bilateralField builders, so they propagate.
  - **Fix:** Snap the 6px label gaps to 8 and the 2px header gap to a scale value (or remove), keeping the field builders compliant since they are reused.
  - **Evidencia:** SizedBox height 6 lines 475, 512; SizedBox height 2 line 636

- **[LOW · consistency]** Date/timezone display inconsistency with the sibling screen. This screen's _formatDateTimeEs (30-37) calls dt.toLocal() and renders local time, while athlete_detail_screen.dart's _formatMeasurementDate (422-425) deliberately renders the stored UTC value with a comment 'display as-is (no .toLocal())'. The header here shows DateTime.now() local at 232/269, but the record is saved as DateTime.now().toUtc() at 181 — the timestamp the trainer sees while logging may not match what the detail screen later shows for the same record. Also both files duplicate the identical _kMonths const (here 14-28; chart 10-24).
  - **Fix:** Align the timezone convention between log and detail screens (pick local or UTC consistently) so the logged timestamp the user sees matches the persisted/displayed one, and lift the duplicated month-abbreviation list into a single shared helper.
  - **Evidencia:** _formatDateTimeEs line 31 (.toLocal()); save recordedAt line 181 (.toUtc()); sibling _formatMeasurementDate lines 422-425; duplicated _kMonths lines 14-28

- **[LOW · navigation]** Primary action label/state is clear (full-width pill, disabled state with spinner), but the disabled reason is invisible. canSave (231) is false when trainerUid is null, yet the button just appears greyed with no explanation; the 'No hay sesión activa' message only appears if the user taps an already-enabled button — when uid is null the button is disabled so that message is effectively unreachable. The user gets a dead, unexplained button.
  - **Fix:** When trainerUid is null, surface a non-blocking inline message near the CTA explaining why saving is unavailable, rather than relying solely on the disabled state.
  - **Evidencia:** canSave line 231; disabled button line 365; unreachable null-session SnackBar lines 164-173

## lib/features/performance/presentation/log_performance_test_screen.dart

_A clean, single-purpose full-screen form for trainers to log a performance test. It fully respects the color and icon design-system rules (zero HEX/Colors.* literals, no direct PhosphorIcons, all colors via AppPalette.of(context)) and its structure is consistent with its sibling log_measurement_screen.dart. The real issues are: (1) every user-facing string is hardcoded Spanish despite a mature 256-key AppL10n system (EN+ES) already shipping analogous keys — a direct violation of the project's own UI rule #3; (2) no client-side validation or error prevention (invalid numeric input is silently dropped, an all-empty form saves an empty record); (3) no unsaved-changes guard on Cancel/swipe-back; and (4) layout/large-type overflow risk in the top bar plus borderline contrast on low-emphasis field labels. None are blocking, but i18n and error-prevention are worth fixing before this pattern is copied further across the Coach module._

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Every user-facing string is hardcoded in Spanish instead of going through AppL10n. Affected: 'Cancelar', 'Cargar evaluación', section labels ('SALTOS (cm)', 'VELOCIDAD (seg)', 'FUERZA 1RM (kg)', 'RESISTENCIA / OTROS', 'NOTAS'), all 17 field labels, the hint 'Observaciones del entrenador…', the CTA 'GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN', and all three snackbar messages ('No hay sesión activa. No se puede guardar.', 'Evaluación guardada', 'No pudimos guardar la evaluación. Probá de nuevo.'). This violates the project's non-negotiable UI rule #3 (docs/design-system.md: 'Nunca hard-code de strings de UI'). The app already has a mature AppL10n system (256 keys, EN + ES) with directly analogous keys that could be reused or extended — e.g. agendaBookingCancel='Cancelar', coachEditorUpdateLabel='GUARDAR CAMBIOS', and an existing 'No pudimos guardar... Probá de nuevo.' error string. The sibling log_measurement_screen.dart has the identical gap, so this is a module-wide debt, not a one-off.
  - **Fix:** Route all strings through AppL10n.of(context), adding performance-specific keys (e.g. performanceLogTitle, performanceSectionJumps, performanceFieldCmj, performanceSaveCta, performanceSavedSnack, performanceSaveErrorSnack, performanceNoSessionSnack) to lib/l10n/app_l10n_es.dart and app_l10n_en.dart. Reuse existing shared keys for 'Cancelar' and the generic save-error copy where wording matches. Do the same pass on log_measurement_screen.dart so the module is consistent.
  - **Evidencia:** Hardcoded strings throughout: line 243 ('Cancelar'), 256 ('Cargar evaluación'), 284/316/348/387/418 (section labels), 287-411 (field labels), 431 (notes hint), 469 ('GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN'), 163/202/210 (snackbars). Contrast: lib/l10n/app_l10n_es.dart already defines agendaBookingCancel, coachEditorUpdateLabel, and 'No pudimos guardar. Probá de nuevo.'

- **[HIGH · usability]** No error prevention or input validation. _parseDouble (line 148) silently converts any unparseable text to null via double.tryParse, so a typo like '12.x.3' is discarded without telling the trainer their value was dropped. There is also no guard against saving a completely empty form: with no fields filled, _save still builds a PerformanceTest with all-null metrics and persists an empty record, and the Save button is enabled as long as a session exists (canSave only checks trainerUid != null && !_saving, line 223). This is a recognition/error-prevention failure (Nielsen): the trainer gets a 'Evaluación guardada' success message for a record that contains no data.
  - **Fix:** Wrap fields in a Form with per-field validators (or live inline error text) that flag non-numeric input and out-of-range values, and disable the Save button (or show a clear message) when no metric field has a value. At minimum, compute 'has at least one non-null metric' and gate canSave on it so empty evaluations can't be saved silently.
  - **Evidencia:** _parseDouble line 148-152 (silent tryParse to null); _save line 156-215 builds and persists regardless of content; canSave line 223 does not check whether any field is filled; success snackbar line 202.

- **[MEDIUM · navigation]** No unsaved-changes protection. The form collects up to 18 fields, but tapping 'Cancelar' (line 239) pops immediately with no confirmation, and because it is pushed as a fullscreenDialog via MaterialPageRoute (athlete_detail_screen.dart line 707-711) the iOS swipe-back / Android system back also dismisses with no PopScope guard. A trainer who fills several metrics and accidentally swipes or taps Cancelar loses all input with no recovery (user control & freedom).
  - **Fix:** Add a PopScope (canPop:false + onPopInvoked) and route the Cancelar button through the same handler, showing a 'Descartar cambios?' confirmation dialog only when at least one field is dirty. Allow immediate pop when the form is pristine so empty-form dismissal stays frictionless.
  - **Evidencia:** Cancelar onPressed line 240-241 pops directly; no PopScope/WillPopScope anywhere in the file; opened with fullscreenDialog (swipe-dismissible) in lib/features/coach/presentation/athlete_detail_screen.dart line 707-711.

- **[MEDIUM · responsive]** Top-bar layout has an overflow risk with large dynamic type and longer localized titles. The Row (line 237) places a 'Cancelar' TextButton, a Spacer, then a right-aligned Column holding the title 'Cargar evaluación' and the date — but the Column is not wrapped in Flexible/Expanded. At large text-scale or once the title is localized (English 'Log evaluation' or a longer label), the title can exceed available width and trigger a RenderFlex overflow, or the date string '$d $m $y · $hh:$mm' can clip. The right-aligned title column also has no maxLines/overflow handling.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the title/date Column in Flexible, give the title maxLines:1 with TextOverflow.ellipsis (or softWrap), and verify the bar at textScaleFactor 1.3–2.0. Consider a standard leading-back / centered-title AppBar pattern to remove the manual Row balancing entirely.
  - **Evidencia:** Row line 237 with TextButton + Spacer + unconstrained Column (line 252-271); title Text line 255-262 and date Text line 263-269 have no maxLines/overflow; date format _formatDateTimeEs line 34-41.

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** Field identity relies entirely on low-contrast 12px labels. Each input's label (e.g. 'CMJ', 'Sprint 10m') is rendered with palette.textMuted, which is white at ~55% alpha (Color(0x8CFFFFFF), app_palette.dart line 70). On the ink background that is roughly 5:1 — acceptable for body text but borderline for the 12px text that is the ONLY identifier of each field, and the field's own hint ('0') and suffix are also textMuted. The numeric value the user types is textPrimary, but the semantic label they navigate by is the muted one. There is also no TextField labelText/Semantics, so a screen reader announces the field by its decoration only; the visual <Text> label above is a separate node not associated with the input.
  - **Fix:** Either raise the field label to textPrimary (or a higher-emphasis token) since it is essential identifying text, or move the label into the InputDecoration (labelText) so it is programmatically associated with the field for screen readers and Flutter's a11y tree. Verify 12px label contrast against WCAG AA at the rendered size.
  - **Evidencia:** _numericField label uses palette.textMuted line 553-557; hint '0' and suffix use textMuted in _inputDecoration line 510/515; textMuted = Color(0x8CFFFFFF) ~55% in app_palette.dart line 70; labels are standalone Text nodes, not InputDecoration labelText.

- **[LOW · design-system]** One spacing value is off the allowed scale. docs/design-system.md restricts spacing to 8·12·14·18·20 ('No usar 4 / 16 / 24'). The gap between each field label and its input uses SizedBox(height: 6) (line 559), which is not on the scale. (The pragmatic 48 button height, 80 bottom spacer, and 8/12/20 paddings elsewhere are within or reasonably adjacent to the scale; 6 is the clear outlier and it repeats on every one of the ~18 fields.)
  - **Fix:** Change the label-to-field gap to 8 to comply with the spacing scale, and apply the same fix in the shared _numericField/_bilateralField builders in log_measurement_screen.dart so the module stays uniform.
  - **Evidencia:** _numericField SizedBox(height: 6) line 559; spacing scale defined in docs/design-system.md line 49.

- **[LOW · states]** The in-button loading spinner has no accompanying status text, and the disabled-state semantics of the Save button are ambiguous. While saving, the CTA collapses to a 20x20 CircularProgressIndicator with no label (line 459-467), so a screen-reader user or anyone glancing at the button gets a bare spinner with no 'Guardando…' context (visibility of system status). Separately, when trainerUid is null the button is permanently disabled with no visible explanation of why the trainer can't save until they tap and get the 'No hay sesión activa' snackbar.
  - **Fix:** Keep the button label visible alongside the spinner (e.g. 'GUARDANDO…' or a Row of spinner + text) and add a Semantics/announce for the saving state. If the disabled state is reachable in practice, surface the reason inline rather than only on tap.
  - **Evidencia:** Saving spinner with no text line 459-467; canSave gating line 223/449; no-session snackbar line 160-167.

## lib/features/profile/presentation/profile_edit_personal_screen.dart (module: profile — "Datos personales" edit screen)

_Solid, well-structured form that already nails the hard parts: AppPalette is used everywhere (zero HEX literals in widgets), all icons go through TreinoIcon, the header/back pattern matches sibling profile screens, save has uploading/saving/error sub-states with snackbar feedback, and there's a proper dirty-check + discard-confirmation dialog. The real gaps are three: (1) almost every user-facing string is hardcoded in Spanish with deferred `// i18n: Fase 6 Etapa 3` markers instead of going through AppL10n — only the validator messages are localized; (2) the initial profile-load AsyncValue is consumed with `whenData` only, so there is no loading or error state — a slow/failed `userProfileProvider` leaves the user staring at a blank form with no spinner, no error, and a save that silently no-ops; (3) accessibility is thin — no Semantics anywhere (icon-only back button, avatar image, edit badge), and several interactive elements are GestureDetectors under the 44pt minimum tap target. Spacing/typography respect the token scale. Findings below are concrete and actionable; the i18n one is partly a known deferral but still a live design-system-rule violation._

- **[HIGH · microcopy-i18n]** Almost every user-facing string on the screen is hardcoded Spanish text marked with `// i18n: Fase 6 Etapa 3`, violating design-system rule #3 (no hard-coded UI strings). This includes the header title 'EDITAR PERFIL' (L364), all field labels 'NOMBRE'/'GÉNERO'/'PESO (KG)'/'ALTURA (CM)'/'EXPERIENCIA' (L398-474), hints 'Tu nombre' (L411), button labels 'DESCARTAR'/'GUARDAR' (L494/505), the gender choices 'HOMBRE'/'MUJER'/'OTRO' (L676-678), the experience labels+descriptions (L734-746), the avatar caption 'Tocá para cambiar tu foto' (L640), the discard dialog title/body/buttons (L287-322), and both error snackbars (L187, L246). Only the three validator messages use AppL10n. The infrastructure already exists — AppL10n is imported and used for validators, and the sibling profile_edit_trainer_screen localizes its title/save/error strings via keys like profileEditTrainerSaveSuccess.
  - **Fix:** Add ARB keys (e.g. profileEditPersonalTitle, profileEditPersonalNameLabel, profileEditPersonalSaveCta, profileEditPersonalDiscardCta, profileEditPersonalGenderMale/Female/Other, profileEditPersonalExperience* , profileEditPersonalAvatarHint, profileEditPersonalDiscardDialogTitle/Body/Confirm/Cancel, profileEditPersonalUploadError, profileEditPersonalSaveError) and resolve them via AppL10n.of(context), mirroring the trainer screen. Keep the warm voseo wording that's already there.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 187, 246, 287, 295, 304, 316, 364, 398-474, 494, 505, 640, 676-746

- **[HIGH · states]** The initial profile load is consumed with `profileAsync.whenData(...)` only (L341) — there is no loading and no error branch. If userProfileProvider has not yet emitted, the user sees the full chrome (header + labels) with empty fields and no spinner or skeleton, with no signal that data is still arriving. If the stream errors, the form stays blank forever and `_save()` falls back to authStateChangesProvider for the uid; if that's also unavailable it sets _SaveState.error (L169) but renders nothing for that error state — the save button just reverts and the user gets no feedback about why nothing happened. This is inconsistent with the sibling profile_edit_trainer_screen, which renders a CircularProgressIndicator while `profile == null` (trainer screen L225-229).
  - **Fix:** Switch to `profileAsync.when(data: ..., loading: ..., error: ...)` (or guard on `valueOrNull == null` like the trainer screen): show a centered CircularProgressIndicator(color: palette.accent) while loading and a localized retry/error message on error. Also surface the `_SaveState.error` case (L169) with a visible message or snackbar so a missing-uid save isn't silent.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 340-349 (whenData only), 168-171 (_SaveState.error never rendered); contrast profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart L225-229

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** No Semantics anywhere on the screen (and none in the entire profile module). Icon-only / image-only interactive elements have no screen-reader labels: the back affordance is an Icon(TreinoIcon.back) inside a GestureDetector (L356-372) with no semantic 'Volver/Atrás' label or button role; the avatar is a tappable circle showing a NetworkImage/FileImage with an edit-pencil badge (L589-637) announced only as a generic image with no 'Cambiar foto de perfil' label or button hint; the gender chips and experience cards are GestureDetectors whose selected state is conveyed only by color, with no `selected` semantic flag.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the back row in Semantics(button: true, label: localized 'Volver'); give the avatar editor Semantics(button: true, label: 'Cambiar foto de perfil'); expose selection state on gender/experience options via Semantics(selected: isSelected, button: true). This matches the flutter-accessibility-audit guidance and the one existing example at workout/.../exercise_slot_row.dart.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 356-372 (back), 589-637 (avatar), 688-711 (gender chips), 756-794 (experience cards); zero Semantics in lib/features/profile/

- **[MEDIUM · accessibility]** Several primary interactive targets are below the 44pt iOS minimum. The header back affordance relies on HitTestBehavior.opaque but the Row's intrinsic height is ~20pt (icon size 20) plus the 18px vertical padding gives a usable band, but the icon itself has no minimum box. The avatar edit badge is a 24x24 indicator (L621-622) — acceptable since the whole 80pt avatar is the tap target. The discard dialog actions are bare TextButtons with default sizing; gender chips are 10px vertical padding around 13px text (~33pt tall, L692) — under 44pt. The pill buttons are correctly 44pt (L822/859).
  - **Fix:** Ensure tappable rows meet 44pt: bump gender chip vertical padding or wrap in a SizedBox(minHeight: 44), and confirm the back icon's hit area is at least 44x44 (e.g. wrap the Icon in a 44pt-min SizedBox or use the padded Row, which currently helps but isn't guaranteed). The 44pt pills are the right reference.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 359-361 (back icon size 20), 690-699 (gender chip vertical 10), vs correct 44pt pills at 822/859

- **[LOW · design-system]** Two minor token deviations. (1) The gender selector uses `Colors.transparent` for the unselected fill (L694) and `_OutlinedPill` uses `Colors.transparent` (L861) — a Colors.* constant rather than an AppPalette token; harmless visually but technically the kind of literal the rules discourage, and AppPalette has no 'transparent' token so it's a gray area. (2) The avatar placeholder/background uses `palette.textMuted.withValues(alpha: 0.12)` (L602) and input borders use `palette.textMuted.withValues(alpha: 0.2)` (L540/547) — ad-hoc alpha math on textMuted instead of the dedicated `palette.border` token (which exists precisely for 1px card borders at 0.10 alpha).
  - **Fix:** Prefer palette.border for the input/avatar outlines instead of textMuted.withValues(alpha: 0.2) to stay on the documented border token. Colors.transparent is acceptable but consider it consistently; not worth a token addition.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 540, 547, 602 (textMuted alpha math); 694, 861 (Colors.transparent)

- **[LOW · usability]** Visibility of system status during save is weak: while saving/uploading the only feedback is the GUARDAR button label changing to '...' (L504) with onTap nulled. There's no spinner, the DESCARTAR button merely disables, and the distinction between 'uploading photo' and 'saving' is invisible to the user even though _SaveState tracks both. The sibling trainer screen shows an actual CircularProgressIndicator inside its save button (trainer L348-356).
  - **Fix:** Replace the '...' label with a small CircularProgressIndicator inside _FilledPill while busy (as the trainer screen does), and optionally differentiate uploading vs saving copy ('Subiendo foto…' / 'Guardando…') so the longer photo-upload step reads as progress, not a hang.
  - **Evidencia:** Lines 484-512 ('...' label), 503-505; contrast profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart L348-356

## lib/features/profile/presentation/profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart (Trainer public-profile edit / onboarding screen)

_The screen is structurally solid on the design-system fundamentals it gets right: colors flow through AppPalette.of(context) with zero HEX literals in widgets, every icon uses TreinoIcon.X, and the save flow has explicit loading/saving/error states plus client-side validation that mirrors the repo's invariants. The real problems cluster in three areas.
