Detail error/not-found use FilledButton (session_detail_screen.dart:283-287, :307-311, labels 'Volver a Entrenar' / 'Reintentar'). Casing contrast vs workoutButtonDone='LISTO' (lib/l10n/app_l10n_es.dart:416).

- **[LOW · accessibility]** The whole history card is a bare GestureDetector with no Semantics label, no button role, and an icon-only back control on the detail screen with no tooltip/semantic label. Screen-reader users get only the concatenated child text for the card and an unlabeled icon for back; the tappable card also isn't announced as actionable.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the card in an InkWell/Semantics with a button label summarizing the session ('Ver sesión: {routine}, {date}'), add a tooltip/semanticLabel to the back IconButton, and give the completed/PR icons text alternatives.
  - **Dónde:** historial_section.dart:182 GestureDetector(onTap: ...) wraps the row with no Semantics; detail back is a plain IconButton with no tooltip (session_detail_screen.dart:82-88); _CompletedIcon and the PR badge convey meaning purely visually.

## Descubrir y contactar trainer (alumno): Trainers list -> trainer public profile -> chat / reservar turno en agenda

_Traced end-to-end across router.dart and the coach/chat modules. The real flow is: Coach tab -> TrainersListScreen (discovery, list/map, Presencial/Online) -> tap tile -> TrainerPublicProfileScreen -> "PEDIR VÍNCULO" (creates a pending trainer_link) -> wait for PF approval -> AthleteCoachView link-state card -> only when ACTIVE do "MENSAJE" (chat) and "VER AGENDA DEL PF" appear. The journey as described ("chat / reservar turno en agenda") does NOT match the product: (1) you cannot contact a trainer directly from the profile — chat is gated behind an accepted link, an asynchronous step the user can't complete on their own; (2) there is NO athlete-side booking at all — the agenda is explicitly READ-ONLY ("The trainer now schedules all sessions; the athlete only views their own"), so "reservar turno" is not a feature. The strongest UX problems are this expectation gap and several dead-ends/feedback gaps in the pending and "already-linked-to-another-PF" states. Files: lib/app/router.dart, lib/features/coach/presentation/trainers_list_screen.dart, trainer_public_profile_screen.dart, athlete_agenda_screen.dart, athlete_coach_view.dart, widgets/trainer_contact_cta_stub.dart, lib/features/chat/presentation/chat_screen.dart. Locale is hardcoded to es_AR (lib/app/locale_resolver.dart), so empty intl_en.arb strings are a latent-only risk._

- **[HIGH · usability]** The primary 'contact' action on the trainer profile is 'PEDIR VÍNCULO' (request a link), not a chat or a booking. The user cannot actually message or book from the profile — contact is gated behind the trainer accepting the link, an asynchronous step the user has no control over. There is no way to chat with a prospective trainer BEFORE committing to a link, which is the most natural first contact action. This is a hidden/blocked primary action: the journey's stated goal ('contactar') cannot be completed at the profile step.
  - **Fix:** Decide what 'contact' means at the profile step and make it match the CTA. Either (a) allow a pre-link inquiry chat from the profile, or (b) if linking is intentionally the only path, rename/reframe the CTA and add a one-line subtitle explaining what happens next ('El PF tiene que aceptar tu solicitud para poder chatear y coordinar sesiones'). Align the journey definition with the product: there is no direct contact-from-profile today.
  - **Dónde:** trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:92 renders TrainerContactCtaStub; the only CTA is coachCtaLabel = 'PEDIR VÍNCULO' (intl_es_AR.arb:66). Chat ('MENSAJE') and agenda only appear in athlete_coach_view.dart:482/590 inside the `link.status == TrainerLinkStatus.active` branch. chat_providers.dart:37 chatForLinkProvider requires a TrainerLink. No chat/contact entry exists on the public profile.

- **[HIGH · usability]** The journey endpoint 'reservar turno en agenda' does not exist for the alumno. The athlete agenda is explicitly READ-ONLY: the screen header is 'VER AGENDA DEL PF' and it only displays the trainer's already-scheduled sessions with no booking, request, or cancel controls. A first-time user who taps 'VER AGENDA DEL PF' expecting to book a slot hits a pure-display calendar — a silent dead-end against intent.
  - **Fix:** If athletes are meant to request/book sessions, add an athlete booking flow (tap free slot -> confirm -> pending request). If booking is intentionally trainer-only, that is a valid model but the journey spec is wrong — the alumno can only chat to coordinate, then the PF schedules. Make the read-only nature obvious before the tap (e.g., 'Tu PF agenda las sesiones — escribile para coordinar') so the user doesn't expect a booking screen.
  - **Dónde:** athlete_agenda_screen.dart:14-16 docstring: 'Full-screen route for the athlete's agenda view — READ-ONLY. The trainer now schedules all sessions; the athlete only views their own.' Day sheet (line 283) 'No booking or cancel controls.' Button label agendaButtonLabel = 'VER AGENDA DEL PF' (intl_es_AR.arb:96). No athlete-side createAppointment/requestSlot exists (grep of lib/features/coach found booking logic only in availability_editor_screen.dart, the trainer's editor).

- **[HIGH · usability]** Dead-end when the athlete already has a link with a DIFFERENT trainer. Browsing other trainers and tapping the CTA shows a disabled button labeled 'YA TENÉS UN PF' with no explanation and no path forward. The user can't tell why they're blocked or what to do (terminate the current link first). Single-PF-at-a-time is a hard constraint surfaced only as a dead, unexplained button.
  - **Fix:** When blocked by an existing link, either keep the button tappable to show an explanatory sheet ('Solo podés tener un PF activo. Terminá tu vínculo actual con {nombre} para pedir uno nuevo.') with a shortcut to the current link, or render an inline helper line under the disabled button. Never leave a disabled primary CTA with an unexplained label.
  - **Dónde:** trainer_contact_cta_stub.dart:124 returns 'YA TENÉS UN PF' as the disabled label; _existingLinkLabel offers no helper text, tooltip, or navigation. disabled state (line 82-89) just nulls onPressed. No SnackBar/dialog explains the one-PF constraint.

- **[MEDIUM · states]** After requesting a link ('Solicitud enviada'), the pending state gives the user no sense of progress or expected timeframe and no proactive notification path described in-flow. The pending card shows 'SOLICITUD ENVIADA' / 'Esperando confirmación' with only a 'CANCELAR SOLICITUD' action. There is no indication of whether/how the user will be told when the PF responds, so the user may repeatedly return to the Coach tab to check. The success SnackBar promises 'Te avisamos cuando el PF responda' but the pending UI doesn't reinforce or fulfil that promise.
  - **Fix:** On the pending card, add a reassuring line ('Te avisaremos por notificación cuando responda') and ideally the request timestamp. Confirm a push/in-app notification actually fires on acceptance; if not, this is a more serious feedback gap (user has no way to know the link was accepted except by manually revisiting).
  - **Dónde:** trainer_contact_cta_stub.dart:57 SnackBar 'Solicitud enviada. Te avisamos cuando el PF responda.'; athlete_coach_view.dart:229 _statusLabel pending = 'SOLICITUD ENVIADA', :287 subtitle 'Esperando confirmación'; _ActionRow pending branch (line 453) only offers 'CANCELAR SOLICITUD'. No ETA, no 'te notificaremos' reinforcement, no status timeline.

- **[MEDIUM · visual-hierarchy]** The most important first-time action in the journey ('PEDIR VÍNCULO') has the weakest visual weight in the flow. It is an OutlinedButton (secondary styling), while the later, less-decisive actions ('MENSAJE') are filled ElevatedButtons (primary styling). The visual hierarchy is inverted relative to the user's goal: the conversion-critical step looks secondary, and a routine messaging action looks primary.
  - **Fix:** Promote 'PEDIR VÍNCULO' to a filled primary button (FilledButton/ElevatedButton with palette.accent) on the public profile so the journey's key conversion step reads as the primary action. Keep destructive/secondary actions (terminar, cancelar) outlined.
  - **Dónde:** trainer_contact_cta_stub.dart:88 OutlinedButton for 'PEDIR VÍNCULO'. athlete_coach_view.dart:482 ElevatedButton.icon (palette.accent fill) for 'MENSAJE'; agenda button (line 589) is outlined. So the entry CTA is outlined while the post-link primary action is filled.

- **[MEDIUM · navigation]** Chat has no persistent entry point in the journey or the app shell — it is reachable ONLY from the 'MENSAJE' button inside the active-link card in AthleteCoachView. A ChatListScreen exists but is not wired into the main bottom-nav shell. Once a conversation exists, the only way back to it is: Coach tab -> link card -> MENSAJE. This buries an ongoing, high-frequency communication channel several taps deep with no top-level affordance.
  - **Fix:** Surface conversations more directly — e.g., a chat/inbox entry on the Coach tab header or the link card, or route ChatListScreen so the athlete can reopen a thread without rebuilding the active-link context each time.
  - **Dónde:** router.dart _kTabs (line 54) = ['/workout','/feed','/home','/coach','/profile'] — no chat tab. Chat route is nested at '/coach/chat/:chatId' (router.dart:408). chat_list_screen.dart exists but is not referenced in router.dart (only chat_screen.dart is imported). Athlete reaches chat via athlete_coach_view.dart:565 context.push from the MENSAJE button.

- **[MEDIUM · states]** Mid-flow failures are handled inconsistently. The trainers list and public profile have retry affordances, but opening the chat on failure only shows a transient SnackBar ('No pudimos abrir el chat. Probá de nuevo.') with no inline retry — the user must re-find and re-tap MENSAJE. The agenda route host renders a raw 'Error: $err' (developer-facing string) on link-resolution failure, leaking internal error text to the user.
  - **Fix:** Standardize error states across the journey: every failure should show a friendly message plus a retry action. Replace the raw 'Error: $err' in the agenda route host with a localized message and a retry. Give the chat-open failure an inline retry instead of a one-shot SnackBar.
  - **Dónde:** athlete_coach_view.dart:568 chat-open failure = SnackBar only, no retry button. router.dart:517 _AthleteAgendaRouteHost error branch: Text('Error: \$err') — raw error object shown to the user. Contrast with trainers_list_screen.dart:309 and trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:45 which provide _ErrorState with onRetry.

- **[LOW · consistency]** Back-navigation and pop semantics differ across the journey's screens, and capitalization of CTAs is inconsistent. Public profile uses context.pop with a /coach fallback; agenda uses Navigator.of(context).pop(); chat uses Navigator.of(context).maybePop(). Button casing mixes ALL-CAPS ('PEDIR VÍNCULO', 'MENSAJE', 'VER AGENDA DEL PF') with sentence-case dialog actions ('Compartir', 'Volver'), and the empty-state CTA on not-found is a hardcoded 'Volver' rather than a localized string.
  - **Fix:** Standardize on go_router's context.pop with a consistent home fallback across all journey screens, and unify CTA casing. Move the hardcoded 'Volver' to the l10n catalog for consistency with the rest of the flow.
  - **Dónde:** trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:37-38 context.canPop()? pop : go('/coach'); athlete_agenda_screen.dart:60 Navigator.of(context).pop(); chat_screen.dart:95 Navigator.of(context).maybePop(). trainer_public_profile_screen.dart:124 hardcoded const Text('Volver') (not l10n) inside _NotFoundState.

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** All English ARB strings for this journey are empty (coachCtaLabel, coachEmptyLabel, agenda*, chat*, etc.). This is currently a latent risk only because resolveLocale hardcodes es_AR regardless of device locale — but the moment English is enabled, the entire journey would render blank labels (empty CTA button, empty empty-state, empty error messages). Several user-facing strings are also hardcoded in Dart rather than localized.
  - **Fix:** Either remove the en locale from the supported set until translated (to avoid shipping blank UI) or populate the en ARB. Migrate the hardcoded Spanish strings in the journey into the ARB so the flow is translation-ready and consistent.
  - **Dónde:** intl_en.arb lines 48-68 all coach/agenda/chat keys = "". lib/app/locale_resolver.dart:17 returns const Locale('es','AR') unconditionally, so en never renders today. Hardcoded Spanish in Dart: trainer_contact_cta_stub.dart:57/124, athlete_coach_view.dart:229-232 status labels, athlete_agenda_screen.dart:333 'No tenés sesiones este día.', chat_screen.dart:269/312/322.

- **[LOW · usability]** Onboarding clarity gap at the discovery entry. A location-permission rationale sheet auto-fires on first open of the trainers list before the user understands the screen, and the Presencial/Online + map/list toggles plus three filter rows present a fair amount of upfront chrome with no first-run guidance on what to do. A first-time user is asked for location permission before they grasp why (to sort by distance).
  - **Fix:** Keep the rationale sheet but ensure its copy ties permission to a clear benefit ('para mostrarte PF cerca tuyo'). Consider a lightweight first-run hint on the discovery screen, and confirm the denied-permission path degrades gracefully (list still usable, distance shows '—'), which the code does handle.
  - **Dónde:** trainers_list_screen.dart:41-60 initState -> addPostFrameCallback -> _maybeShowRationale shows LocationPermissionRationaleSheet immediately on first build. The body stacks _ModeTabs, list/map toggle, ESPECIALIDAD chips, and FILTROS chips (lines 88-120) with no empty-flow hint beyond the no-results _EmptyState.

## Coach gestiona disponibilidad y agenda (Coach screen → availability editor → athlete detail / agenda)

_Traced the trainer journey end-to-end. Entry: CoachScreen renders TrainerCoachView with two segmented sub-tabs (ALUMNOS / AGENDA). The AGENDA tab (trainer_agenda_tab.dart) shows a "NUEVA SESIÓN" CTA + month/week calendar + inline DayTimeline; tapping a block opens SessionDetailSheet (notes, cancel, cancel-series), tapping empty space opens NewSessionSheet. The availability editor (availability_editor_screen.dart) manages weekly rules + date overrides via /coach/availability-editor. Athlete detail is reached from the session sheet's athlete row or the ALUMNOS tab. The single biggest journey problem is structural: the availability editor — the step explicitly named in the journey — is NOT linked from the Coach/AGENDA flow at all. It is reachable ONLY from a separate Profile tab row ("Disponibilidad", bell icon), breaking the journey into two disconnected surfaces. Feedback is good in the session/notes flows (loading spinners + success/error SnackBars) but absent or actively misleading in the availability editor, where save errors are silently swallowed. Terminology and button styling are mostly consistent, but the editor diverges (Material back arrow + AppBar vs the rest of the module's sheet/pill language) and uses raw Material icons instead of TreinoIcon._

- **[HIGH · navigation]** The availability editor — the central step of this journey — has NO entry point inside the Coach/AGENDA flow. The only way to reach it is from a completely different tab (Profile → 'Disponibilidad' row). A trainer working in the AGENDA tab who wants to set up their bookable hours has no affordance to do so; they must leave to Profile and hunt for it. The doc comment in trainer_agenda_tab.dart (line 16) even claims the tab lets the trainer 'See their availability rules summary + navigate to availability editor', but build() contains neither a rules summary nor any link — the documented design was never implemented (or was removed).
  - **Fix:** Add a visible availability entry point inside the AGENDA tab — e.g. a 'Mis horarios' summary card or a header IconButton next to NUEVA SESIÓN that pushes the editor. This keeps 'configure when I'm bookable' and 'see/book my agenda' in one coherent surface and fixes the journey discontinuity. Also delete or correct the stale doc comment.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/trainer_agenda_tab.dart line 16 (stale doc) vs the actual build() at lines 57-145 (no availability link/summary). Real entry point: lib/features/profile/trainer_profile_view.dart lines 114-121 (context.push('/coach/availability-editor?trainerId=$uid')).

- **[HIGH · states]** In the availability editor, both save paths silently swallow errors AND give no success feedback. _RuleFormSheet._save and _BlockOverrideFormSheet._save wrap the repository call in `catch (_) { // ignore }` and pop the sheet on success with no SnackBar. On a network/permission failure the sheet closes exactly as if the save succeeded — the trainer believes a rule/override was created when it was not, then later sees athletes can't book and has no idea why. This is a Nielsen 'visibility of system status' + 'error prevention' failure at the most consequential step (publishing availability).
  - **Fix:** Mirror the pattern already used in new_session_sheet.dart and session_detail_sheet.dart: on success show a confirmation SnackBar ('Horario guardado.'); on catch, keep the sheet open, reset _saving, and show 'No pudimos guardar. Probá de nuevo.' Never pop on a swallowed error.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/availability_editor_screen.dart: _save lines 530-573 ('// ignore save errors in this phase', pop with no SnackBar) and _BlockOverrideFormSheet._save lines 699-715 ('// ignore').

- **[MEDIUM · states]** The availability editor collapses load failures into the empty state. Rules and overrides are read with `valueOrNull ?? const []`, so a stream error renders the exact same 'Sin horarios configurados' / 'Sin excepciones' hint as a genuinely empty list. A trainer who actually has rules but hits a transient error is told they have none — and the empty hint invites them to re-create rules that may already exist (risk of duplicates).
  - **Fix:** Handle the AsyncValue error/loading states explicitly: show a skeleton/spinner while loading and a retry-able error message on error, distinct from the empty state — consistent with how the ALUMNOS tab handles linksAsync.when(loading/error/data).
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/availability_editor_screen.dart lines 78-79 (rulesAsync.valueOrNull ?? const []; overridesAsync.valueOrNull ?? const []) feeding the rules.isEmpty / overrides.isEmpty branches at lines 87-111.

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** The rule editor lets the trainer create overlapping or duplicate weekly rules with no validation or warning. The only check is window >= one slot duration; two rules for the same day with overlapping hours (or identical rules) are both accepted. This produces confusing or double-counted bookable slots downstream and the trainer gets no feedback that the schedule is inconsistent.
  - **Fix:** Before saving, check the new/edited rule against existing rules for the same dayOfWeek and warn on overlap or exact duplicate (block, or confirm-to-merge). At minimum surface a 'Ya tenés un horario que se superpone' message.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/availability_editor_screen.dart _save lines 530-566 — only the endTotalMinutes < startTotalMinutes + slot check exists before addRule/updateRule; no comparison against existing rules.

- **[MEDIUM · consistency]** The availability editor breaks the visual and interaction language used everywhere else in the journey. Every other surface (agenda, session sheets, new-session, athlete cards) uses TreinoIcon.* and the sheet/pill/StadiumBorder language; the editor uses raw Material icons (Icons.arrow_back, Icons.edit_outlined, Icons.delete_outline, Icons.calendar_today_outlined, Icons.access_time_outlined) and a standard AppBar with a back arrow. This violates the project rule 'Use TreinoIcon.X — never PhosphorIcons/Material directly' and makes the editor feel like a different app, weakening the sense of one continuous flow.
  - **Fix:** Swap raw Material icons for TreinoIcon equivalents and align the editor's chrome (back affordance, button shapes) with the module's existing pill/sheet styling so the journey reads as one consistent experience.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/availability_editor_screen.dart lines 43 (Icons.arrow_back), 272 (Icons.edit_outlined), 278 & 352 (Icons.delete_outline), 642 (Icons.calendar_today_outlined), 883 (Icons.access_time_outlined). Compare new_session_sheet.dart which uses TreinoIcon.plus/calendar/clock/chevronDown.

- **[MEDIUM · microcopy-i18n]** The single most important label in the journey is mislabeled. The availability entry point in Profile reads 'Disponibilidad' with a BELL icon (TreinoIcon.bell). A bell universally signals notifications/reminders, so trainers are unlikely to recognize this as 'set my bookable hours'. Additionally the brand naming convention (Coach = PF module) isn't reflected; nothing in the row ties it to the agenda concept the trainer is looking for.
  - **Fix:** Use a calendar/clock icon (e.g. TreinoIcon.calendar or clock) and consider a clearer label such as 'Mis horarios de trabajo' (which the editor itself already uses as its section header) so the entry point matches the destination's own wording.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/profile/trainer_profile_view.dart lines 114-121: _MenuRow(icon: TreinoIcon.bell, label: 'Disponibilidad', ...).

- **[MEDIUM · microcopy-i18n]** Hardcoded Spanish strings are mixed with localized (l10n) strings within the same journey, an inconsistency that will break the moment a second locale is added and signals the flow was half-migrated. The editor localizes the title and CTAs via AppL10n but hardcodes section headers and labels ('MIS HORARIOS DE TRABAJO', 'EXCEPCIONES', 'Sin excepciones.', '¿Eliminar esta excepción?', 'Editar horario', 'Día de la semana', 'Hora inicio', 'Fecha a bloquear'). New-session and session-detail sheets have the same mix.
  - **Fix:** Move all user-facing strings in the journey to AppL10n so terminology stays consistent and the flow is locale-ready.
  - **Dónde:** availability_editor_screen.dart hardcoded: lines 85, 90-91, 109, 111, 200, 428, 438, 448, 462, 476, 629 vs localized AppL10n.of(context) at lines 47, 102, 120, 154-163, 516. session_detail_sheet.dart hardcodes 'CANCELAR TODA LA SERIE', 'GUARDAR NOTAS', 'ANTES DE LA SESIÓN' (lines 335, 418, 471) alongside l10n calls.

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Day timeline has no empty state. When the selected day has zero sessions the DayTimeline renders only a bare hour grid (lines + hour labels) with no message. A first-time trainer who hasn't booked anything sees an empty ruled grid with no guidance that they can tap to create a session or that the day is simply free, leaving the primary 'tap empty area to add' affordance entirely hidden.
  - **Fix:** When the day has no sessions, overlay a subtle hint (e.g. 'Día libre — tocá un horario para agregar una sesión') so the empty grid communicates both state and the available action.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/widgets/day_timeline.dart — sessions filtered at lines 108-114, but build() only ever renders grid + blocks + now-line; no branch for sessions.isEmpty produces a hint. The tap-to-create gesture (lines 182-198) is invisible.

- **[LOW · states]** The recurring-session creation path can produce a confusing partial-silent outcome. createRecurringByTrainer returns a count; count==0 shows a helpful message, but a partial result (e.g. some occurrences collided with existing bookings or fell in the past) is reported only as 'N sesiones registradas' with no indication that fewer than requested were created. The trainer can't tell the difference between 'all 4 weeks booked' and 'only 2 of the requested slots were created'.
  - **Fix:** If the created count is less than the expected number of occurrences (weekdays × weeks minus past), surface a 'Se crearon N de M sesiones (algunas estaban ocupadas o en el pasado)' message so the trainer knows the schedule is incomplete.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/widgets/new_session_sheet.dart _submitRecurring lines 472-509 — only count==0 is special-cased; any count>0 reports success without comparing to the expected number.

- **[LOW · usability]** Cancellation rules are enforced but not explained ahead of time, creating a mild dead-end. A session within 24h shows 'No se puede cancelar (menos de 24h).' only after the trainer opens the sheet, and the editor/agenda give no earlier signal. For a trainer needing to free a slot last-minute this is a hard stop with no alternative path offered (e.g. contact athlete, mark as no-show).
  - **Fix:** Either expose the 24h policy proactively (badge on near-term sessions) or offer a fallback action when cancellation is blocked (open chat with the athlete, or a 'marcar ausente' option), so the trainer isn't left at a dead-end.
  - **Dónde:** lib/features/coach/presentation/widgets/session_detail_sheet.dart lines 183-186 (canCancel / isWithin24h) and 448-457 (the muted dead-end message); CancellationTooLateException handling at lines 102-106.

- **[LOW · consistency]** Confirm-dialog button semantics are inconsistent across the journey for destructive actions. In trainer_coach_view.dart the destructive 'Terminar vínculo' confirm uses an accent-colored confirm button (palette.accent) while session cancellation in session_detail_sheet uses palette.highlight, and the editor's delete confirm uses palette.accent for a destructive delete. Destructive confirmations don't reliably read as destructive, weakening error prevention.
  - **Fix:** Standardize: destructive confirms (delete rule/override, cancel reserva, terminate link) should consistently use a danger/highlight color, non-destructive confirms the accent color, across all dialogs in the journey.
  - **Dónde:** trainer_coach_view.dart _confirmAndRun ElevatedButton uses confirmBg (accent for pause/resume, highlight for terminate, lines 269-343); availability_editor_screen.dart _ConfirmDialog confirm button is palette.accent (lines 946-959) even for delete; session_detail_sheet _localConfirmDialog uses palette.highlight (lines 534-547).

## Coach Hub: subir y asignar plan (login -> dashboard -> upload plan (excel) -> plan preview -> asignar a alumno)

_Traced the full Coach Hub plan-import journey across 4 screens + router (lib/app/coach_hub_router.dart, coach_hub_login_screen.dart, coach_hub_dashboard_screen.dart, coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart, coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart, plus plan_import_repository.dart / excel_parser.dart for failure paths). The happy path is coherent and well-instrumented (loading spinners, snackbars, analytics on assign). The most serious problems are around navigation and work-loss: every step uses context.go() (route replacement), so there is no back stack and going back from the preview silently discards the parsed plan and all manual exercise mappings. The unmatched-exercise recovery story is internally contradictory (a warning tells the PF to re-upload the Excel while the day cards offer inline manual mapping). The athlete picker reads a deprecated non-realtime provider, so an athlete accepting mid-flow won't appear without a manual reload. There is also no per-student 'assign plan' entry point and no success confirmation that survives the redirect to a near-identical-looking dashboard._

- **[HIGH · usability]** Navigating back from the Preview screen silently destroys all work. The preview '_Header' back button and the upload '_Header' back button both call context.go() (route replacement, not push). The parsed plan lives in the ephemeral autoDispose parsedPlanProvider; when the PF taps back from preview to '/upload-plan', the upload screen state is rebuilt fresh and any manually-mapped 'sin match' exercises (resolved one by one in the preview via the bottom sheet) are lost. Re-entering preview with a stale/null plan triggers the post-frame redirect back to '/upload-plan'. A PF who spent minutes resolving 8 unmatched exercises loses all of it with one back tap and no warning.
  - **Fix:** Either (a) warn before leaving preview when manual mappings exist / the plan is non-empty (showDialog confirm), or (b) persist the parsed+mapped plan so back-and-forward is non-destructive, and use push/pop so the browser/system back button maps to a real stack. At minimum, do not silently drop a fully-resolved plan.
  - **Dónde:** coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:361 IconButton onPressed: () => context.go('/upload-plan'); parsedPlanProvider is autoDispose StateProvider; manual mappings written via ref.read(parsedPlanProvider.notifier).state = current.copyWith(...) at lines 171-174. coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart:193 also uses context.go('/dashboard').

- **[HIGH · navigation]** The entire journey uses context.go() exclusively, so there is no navigation stack. On web (Coach Hub is desktop-first web), the browser Back button and forward button do not behave like step-back through upload->preview; go() replaces the location. Combined with the autoDispose plan state, the browser Back button mid-flow is a dead-end / data-loss trap rather than a safe 'previous step'.
  - **Fix:** Model upload->preview as pushed sub-steps (context.push) so pop() returns to the previous step with state intact, and the web Back button works as users expect. Keep go() only for terminal transitions (login->dashboard, success->dashboard).
  - **Dónde:** All transitions are context.go: dashboard->upload (coach_hub_dashboard_screen.dart:168), upload->preview (coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart:90), preview back (coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:361), preview->dashboard on success (line 119), upload back (coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart:193). No GoRouter.push / context.push anywhere in the flow; router has no nested routes for proper pop.

- **[HIGH · consistency]** Contradictory error-recovery guidance for unmatched exercises. The _UnmatchedWarning banner tells the PF: 'Ajustá los nombres en el Excel y volvé a subirlo. No se puede asignar hasta que estén todos resueltos.' But each unmatched row ALSO renders an inline 'Asignar manualmente' button that opens an exercise-picker sheet and resolves the match in place. The two recovery paths conflict: the banner implies the only fix is editing the spreadsheet and re-uploading (which, per the navigation finding, destroys other progress), while the actual supported path is inline mapping. A first-time PF will follow the banner, re-upload, and lose work unnecessarily.
  - **Fix:** Rewrite the warning to point to the inline action: 'Tenés N ejercicios sin match. Resolvelos con "Asignar manualmente" en cada uno, o corregí los nombres en el Excel.' Make the primary recovery (inline mapping) the one the copy emphasizes.
  - **Dónde:** Banner copy at coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:508-516. Inline 'Asignar manualmente' TextButton at lines 597-617 (onPickManual -> _pickExerciseFor -> _ExercisePickerSheet). The assign guard at lines 65-69 blocks on plan.unmatched.isNotEmpty regardless of which path is used.

- **[MEDIUM · states]** Athlete picker uses the DEPRECATED non-realtime provider, so the list can be stale during the flow. linksForTrainerProvider is explicitly @Deprecated in favor of trainerLinksStreamProvider precisely so transitions (incl. accept) reflect without manual invalidate. In the preview, if an athlete accepts the trainer's link request while the PF is on the preview screen, the new active athlete will NOT appear in 'ASIGNAR A' until the provider re-fetches (autoDispose, but no live stream). The dashboard itself uses the stream provider, creating an inconsistency between what the dashboard shows and what the picker offers.
  - **Fix:** Switch _AthletePicker to trainerLinksStreamProvider (filter status==active) so the assignable list is realtime and consistent with the dashboard, and remove the deprecated dependency from this flow.
  - **Dónde:** coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:830 ref.watch(linksForTrainerProvider(trainerId)). Provider marked @Deprecated('Use trainerLinksStreamProvider for real-time updates') at trainer_link_providers.dart:23-33. Dashboard uses trainerLinksStreamProvider (coach_hub_dashboard_screen.dart:298).

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Missing per-student entry point to assign a plan. The dashboard lists active students with 'Pausar' and 'Terminar vínculo' actions, but the only way to assign a plan is the single global 'IMPORTAR PLAN DESDE EXCEL' button at the top, after which the PF must re-find and select the student in the preview's multi-select picker. The natural mental model ('assign a plan to THIS student') has no affordance from the student tile. This adds friction and makes single-athlete assignment indirect.
  - **Fix:** Add an 'Asignar plan' action on each active _StudentTile that routes to /upload-plan with the athlete pre-selected (pass athleteId), so the picker is pre-populated. Keep the global import for bulk multi-athlete assignment.
  - **Dónde:** Dashboard _StudentTile actions are only Pausar / Terminar (coach_hub_dashboard_screen.dart:539-548). Sole assign entry is the top ElevatedButton (lines 167-184). The assign target is chosen at the very end in the preview picker (coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:816-887).

- **[MEDIUM · states]** Success feedback is fragile and easy to miss. After assigning, the only confirmation is a SnackBar shown right before context.go('/dashboard'). Showing a snackbar and immediately replacing the route can cause the snackbar to be dismissed/cut by the navigation, and the destination dashboard looks almost identical to where the flow started, with no 'plan assigned to X' marker or any indication on the student tile that a plan now exists. The PF gets no durable confirmation that the assignment landed.
  - **Fix:** Surface the confirmation on the destination (e.g., dashboard reads a one-shot 'just assigned' flag and shows a persistent banner), and/or show plan status on the student tile ('Plan activo: <name>'). Avoid relying on a snackbar that competes with a route replacement.
  - **Dónde:** coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:116-119 ScaffoldMessenger.showSnackBar(...) immediately followed by context.go('/dashboard'). Dashboard student tiles show only 'Vinculado desde DD/MM/YYYY' (line 529), never plan/assignment status.

- **[MEDIUM · states]** Partial-failure on multi-athlete assignment leaves the PF in an ambiguous, unrecoverable state. _assign loops over selected athletes; if some createAssigned calls fail, it shows 'Plan asignado a N atleta(s). M fallaron.' then clears the plan (parsedPlanProvider=null) and navigates to the dashboard regardless. The PF cannot see WHICH athletes failed and has no retry path for just the failed ones, the parsed plan is already gone, and the message disappears with the navigation.
  - **Fix:** On partial failure, stay on the preview, keep the plan, mark the failed athletes in the picker, and offer a 'Reintentar con los que fallaron' action. Only clear state and navigate once everything succeeded or the PF explicitly abandons.
  - **Dónde:** coach_hub_plan_preview_screen.dart:81-119: failed list collected per-athlete; only if ALL fail does it stay on screen (lines 101-107); on partial success it clears state at line 109 and go('/dashboard') at line 119 with a transient snackbar naming counts but not names.

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Stated file constraints (.xlsx, 10 MB) are not actually enforced or fed back. The upload card says 'Archivo .xlsx, hasta 10 MB.' The picker restricts extensions to xlsx, but there is no size check anywhere; a >10MB file is accepted, then either silently processed or fails with a generic 'No pudimos procesar el archivo' rather than 'el archivo supera 10 MB'. The constraint is advisory only, so the feedback for violating it is wrong/generic.
  - **Fix:** Validate size in _pickFile (reject >10MB with a specific message) so the stated limit is real and the error names the actual cause.
  - **Dónde:** Copy at coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart:333 ('Archivo .xlsx, hasta 10 MB.'). _pickFile (lines 36-45) sets allowedExtensions ['xlsx'] but never checks result.files.first.size. _processFile (lines 69-104) has no size guard; large/invalid bytes fall to the generic catch at lines 97-103.

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** Excel validation errors are precise but surface raw spreadsheet jargon mid-flow without guiding the fix, and appear below the fold. Messages like 'Día 2, fila 7: faltan series.' are good, but they render as a single red line at the bottom of the upload screen (below both cards), and the PF has no link back to where the template defines columns. For a first-time PF this is the riskiest comprehension moment of the journey and the help (template card) is above, already scrolled past.
  - **Fix:** Render parse errors inside/next to the Upload card (not far below), and when a parse error occurs, re-surface the 'Descargar template' affordance with copy like 'Revisá el formato — descargá el template de referencia.'
  - **Dónde:** Validation messages thrown in excel_parser.dart (e.g. lines 162-164, 188-189, 223-228) surface via PlanImportException -> _error Text at coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart:135-142, rendered after both cards.

- **[LOW · navigation]** No way to abandon the import cleanly from the upload step other than 'Volver', and dashboard sign-out has no confirmation. Minor, but the journey lacks a consistent 'Cancelar import' affordance; the back arrow is the only exit, and there's no indication the in-progress picked file will be discarded.
  - **Fix:** Add an explicit 'Cancelar' label semantics to the back action on upload/preview, and consider a lightweight confirm on sign-out for consistency with the destructive-action confirms used elsewhere (Pausar/Terminar).
  - **Dónde:** Upload screen exit is only the _Header back arrow (coach_hub_upload_plan_screen.dart:192-196). Dashboard 'Salir' signs out immediately with no confirm (coach_hub_dashboard_screen.dart:148-153).

## Feed social: Feed → crear post → buscar usuarios → friend requests → public profile

_Traced the full social journey end-to-end across the feed module (lib/features/feed) plus the profile tab. Screens: FeedScreen (feed_screen.dart), CreatePostScreen (create_post_screen.dart + create_post_notifier.dart), SearchUsersScreen (search_users_screen.dart + search_users_provider.dart), PublicProfileScreen (public_profile_screen.dart) where requests are SENT via PublicProfileFollowButton, and FriendRequestsInboxScreen (friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart) where requests are RECEIVED. The flow is functional and the state machine for the follow button is well thought out, but it has three structural problems: (1) the inbox where you accept/reject requests is NOT reachable from anywhere in the feed/search flow — it lives only under the Profile tab, so the loop \"send request → other accepts → manage incoming\" is broken from the social surface; (2) almost no positive feedback — posting a successful post, sending a friend request, and accepting/rejecting requests all happen silently with no confirmation; (3) several mutation errors are swallowed entirely (accept/reject/unfriend), leaving the user with no signal that an action failed. Secondary issues: inconsistent navigation semantics (go vs push) that break back-stack expectations, inconsistent back icons, non-functional stub buttons presented as real controls (MENSAJE, ETIQUETAR RUTINA), and empty states with no call-to-action._

- **[HIGH · navigation]** The friend-requests inbox (where the user ACCEPTS or REJECTS incoming requests) is unreachable from the entire feed/search/profile-viewing flow. It is registered at /profile/friend-requests and the ONLY navigation to it is the 'Solicitudes de amistad' tile inside the Profile tab's CUENTA section. Nothing in FeedScreen, SearchUsersScreen, or PublicProfileScreen links to it. The social loop is therefore broken: after person A sends a request from a public profile, person B has no path from the social surface (Feed/Search) to act on it — they must independently discover it deep inside the Profile tab.
  - **Fix:** Surface a requests entry point on the Feed surface itself — e.g. an inbox/bell icon in the _FeedHeader (next to search and the + button) that badges pendingRequestCountProvider, routing to the inbox. This closes the send→receive→act loop without forcing users to hunt through the Profile tab.
  - **Dónde:** lib/app/router.dart:433-435 nests friend-requests under /profile. Only entry point: lib/features/profile/presentation/widgets/profile_cuenta_section.dart:56 context.push('/profile/friend-requests'). FeedScreen header (feed_screen.dart:122-140) exposes only search + create buttons — no requests/notifications affordance. grep for navigation into friend-requests returns exactly one hit, in the profile section.

- **[HIGH · states]** No success feedback anywhere in the journey's mutating actions. Publishing a post simply pops the screen (create_post_screen.dart:172 'if (ok) context.pop()') with no toast/snackbar confirming success. Sending a friend request (SEGUIR) only swaps the pill label to 'SOLICITUD ENVIADA' — fine on the profile, but the user gets zero acknowledgment that anything was sent. Accept/Reject in the inbox just makes the row vanish via stream re-emission. The app HAS a root ScaffoldMessenger (app.dart:29,93) used for push notifications, so the infrastructure for snackbars exists but is not used for these user-initiated actions.
  - **Fix:** Add a brief success snackbar via the existing root ScaffoldMessenger after: post published ('Post publicado'), request sent ('Solicitud enviada'), and request accepted ('Ahora son amigos'). At minimum the post-publish case, since the user is ejected from the compose screen with no trace of what happened.
  - **Dónde:** create_post_screen.dart:170-173 (submit → pop, no confirmation). public_profile_follow_button.dart:50-57 (request, no feedback). friend_request_inbox_tile.dart:142-169 (_onAceptar: row disappears, no confirmation). No ScaffoldMessenger/SnackBar usage in any feed screen (grep confirmed hits only in coach_hub and coach modules, plus app.dart push handler).

- **[HIGH · states]** Friendship mutation errors are silently swallowed, producing dead-ends with no recovery path. On accept/reject in the inbox, a thrown error is caught and discarded with only a comment ('Swallow — stream will not emit a removal, so row stays'); the row just stays put with no error message, so the user re-taps a button that appears to do nothing. The unfriend confirmation does the same (delete error swallowed). On the public profile, ACCEPT and SEGUIR taps are not wrapped in try/catch at all and have no loading state — a failed network write leaves the pill unchanged with no spinner and no error.
  - **Fix:** Show an error snackbar on caught failures (retry-able) instead of swallowing, and add an in-flight disabled/spinner state to the public-profile SEGUIR/ACEPTAR pills (the inbox tile already has a _busy guard — mirror it on the profile button). Silent failure on a social action is the worst kind: the user assumes success.
  - **Dónde:** friend_request_inbox_tile.dart:164-166 and 184-186 (catch (_) {} with explanatory comment). public_profile_follow_button.dart:120-123 (delete error swallowed). public_profile_follow_button.dart:50-57 and 79-88 (request/accept: bare await repo.request/accept, no try/catch, no busy state on the pill).

- **[MEDIUM · navigation]** Inconsistent navigation semantics between equivalent author/profile taps. Tapping a post author in the feed uses context.go('/feed/profile/...') (REPLACES the feed in the stack), while tapping a search result or an inbox requester uses context.push('/feed/profile/...') (PUSHES on top). Same destination (public profile), two different back-stack behaviors: from the feed, pressing back after viewing a profile does NOT return to the feed list scroll position as a pushed route would — it re-enters the feed fresh. This makes the back button behave unpredictably depending on where the user came from.
  - **Fix:** Use context.push consistently for author/profile navigation from the feed so the public profile is a proper modal-stack push and back returns to the exact feed state. Reserve go for tab switches.
  - **Dónde:** feed_screen.dart:175,233,286 use context.go for onAuthorTap. search_users_screen.dart:271 uses context.push. friend_request_inbox_tile.dart:73 uses context.push. All target the same /feed/profile/:uid route.

- **[LOW · consistency]** Back affordance is inconsistent across the journey's sub-screens. SearchUsersScreen uses the raw Material Icons.arrow_back, while FriendRequestsInboxScreen uses the design-system TreinoIcon.back, and CreatePostScreen uses no back icon at all — instead a text 'CANCELAR' button. Three screens in the same flow, three different dismiss patterns. The raw Icons.arrow_back in search also violates the project rule to use TreinoIcon.X rather than Material/Phosphor icons directly (CLAUDE.md / AGENTS.md).
  - **Fix:** Standardize on TreinoIcon.back for all back headers in the flow (fixes both the visual inconsistency and the icon-system rule violation). Decide intentionally whether compose should use a back chevron or 'CANCELAR' and apply it consistently.
  - **Dónde:** search_users_screen.dart:116 Icon(Icons.arrow_back). friend_requests_inbox_screen.dart:105 Icon(TreinoIcon.back). create_post_screen.dart:144-152 text 'CANCELAR'. The close icon in search (close suffix, line 190) is also Icons.close.

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Non-functional stub controls are presented as real, tappable UI within the journey, inviting taps that do nothing. The public profile shows a 'MENSAJE' button next to the working follow button (opacity 0.6, onTap null) and a 'RUTINAS PÚBLICAS'/'ACTIVIDAD' tab area whose bodies always read 'Aún no hay rutinas públicas' / 'Aún no hay actividad reciente' regardless of the user. The compose screen shows an 'ETIQUETAR RUTINA' chip (opacity 0.4, onTap null). A first-time user cannot tell these are 'coming soon' vs. genuinely empty/broken — the MENSAJE button in particular looks like a primary action.
  - **Fix:** Either hide stub controls until implemented, or label them explicitly (e.g. 'MENSAJE · pronto') so their disabled state reads as intentional. Showing a dead primary-looking 'MENSAJE' button on every profile erodes trust in the whole surface.
  - **Dónde:** public_profile_screen.dart:109-142 _MessageButtonStub (onTap null). public_profile_screen.dart:231-249 _ProfileTabBody hardcoded placeholder copy. create_post_screen.dart:412-449 _RoutineTagStubChip (onTap null).

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Empty states across the journey are dead-ends with no call-to-action. The Feed AMIGOS tab shows 'Aún no hay posts de tus amigos' but offers no button to find/add friends — the user must independently realize the search icon in the header is how to build a friend network. Search initial state ('Buscá usuarios por nombre') and no-results state are pure text. FeedEmptyState renders only an icon + message, no action slot.
  - **Fix:** For the AMIGOS empty state especially, add a 'Buscar usuarios' CTA that routes to /feed/search — this is the single highest-leverage onboarding nudge for the social loop. Extend FeedEmptyState with an optional action widget.
  - **Dónde:** feed_screen.dart:157-160 (amigos empty). feed_empty_state.dart:7-40 (no action parameter at all). search_users_screen.dart:229,233 (initial/below-min states are plain text).

- **[LOW · states]** The post character limit is enforced inconsistently and gives weak feedback. The counter turns red when over kMaxPostChars (280) and canSubmit becomes false, but the TextField has no maxLength and nothing stops typing far past the limit; the only signal is the small red 'N / 280' counter and the PUBLICAR button silently dimming to opacity 0.4. A user who pastes a long text sees the button greyed with no explanation of WHY they can't publish.
  - **Fix:** When over the limit, surface an explicit inline message (reuse the existing _InlineError pattern) such as 'Te pasaste por N caracteres' so the dimmed PUBLICAR has a visible cause.
  - **Dónde:** create_post_screen.dart:218-240 (_PostTextField has maxLines null but no maxLength). create_post_notifier.dart:35-38 canSubmit checks length <= kMaxPostChars. create_post_screen.dart:166-167 button opacity 0.4 when !canSubmit, with no helper text tying it to the over-limit reason.

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** Search requires a minimum of 2 characters (kSearchMinChars) but the below-minimum state shows the SAME copy as the empty/initial state ('Buscá usuarios por nombre'). A user who types one character sees no indication that they need to keep typing — it looks identical to having typed nothing, which can read as 'search is broken' for short names.
  - **Fix:** Differentiate the below-min state, e.g. 'Escribí al menos 2 letras', so the gate is discoverable rather than appearing inert.
  - **Dónde:** search_users_screen.dart:228-234: both activeQuery.isEmpty and activeQuery.length < kSearchMinChars return the identical FeedEmptyState('Buscá usuarios por nombre').

## Perfil y cuenta (Profile → editar personal → gym → rutinas → editar perfil trainer → eliminar cuenta)

_The journey is functional and the high-stakes endpoint (eliminar cuenta) is excellent: re-auth sheet, loading overlay, error SnackBar with retry, and a deterministic redirect to /welcome. But the path leading to it is inconsistent and uneven on feedback. Two screens (edit-personal, gym) give NO success feedback after saving — they just pop, leaving the user unsure the change persisted — while trainer-edit shows a success SnackBar; this is the most repeated friction in the flow. The gym screen has NO error handling on save (a network failure silently leaves the user on the screen with the spinner gone and nothing changed — a dead-end). The unsaved-changes guard on edit-personal only covers the in-app back row, not iOS swipe-back / Android system back (no PopScope), so edits are silently lost — notable given the active branch is fix/workout-swipe-back. There are three different header/back patterns and three different save-button styles across the four sub-screens, plus an asymmetry where 'Cerrar sesión' fires instantly with no confirmation while 'Eliminar cuenta' (its neighbor) is heavily guarded. Trainer-edit is the only screen built on Scaffold+AppBar; the rest are bare Columns. Findings below cite each step._

- **[HIGH · states]** After a successful save in 'Datos personales' (editar personal) and 'Gimnasio' (gym), the screen simply pops back to the hub with NO success confirmation (no SnackBar, toast, or visible state change). The user cannot tell whether the save succeeded or the screen was just dismissed. This is inconsistent with the trainer-edit screen, which DOES show a success SnackBar (profileEditTrainerSaveSuccess).
  - **Fix:** Show a success SnackBar on the hub after editar-personal and gym save (e.g. 'Cambios guardados' / 'Gimnasio actualizado'), matching the trainer-edit pattern. Because the screen pops immediately, surface it via a result flag the hub reads, or show it before popping. Make success feedback uniform across all three edit screens.
  - **Dónde:** profile_edit_personal_screen.dart _save(): `await ref.read(userRepositoryProvider).update(uid, partial); if (mounted) context.pop();` — no success message. profile_gym_screen.dart _save(): `await ...update(uid, {'gymId': gymId}); if (mounted) context.pop();` — no success message. Contrast profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart line 200: shows ScaffoldMessenger SnackBar(profileEditTrainerSaveSuccess) before navigating.

- **[HIGH · states]** The Gimnasio (gym) save has NO error handling. The try block has only a finally that resets the spinner — there is no catch. On a network/permission failure the spinner disappears, the screen stays put, no error is shown, and (since context.pop() is inside the try) the screen does NOT pop. The user is stranded with no feedback and no way to know the save failed: a silent dead-end.
  - **Fix:** Add a catch that shows an error SnackBar ('No pudimos guardar el gimnasio. Probá de nuevo.') and keeps the form editable, mirroring editar-personal's catch on line 241-253. Without it, every gym-change failure is invisible.
  - **Dónde:** profile_gym_screen.dart _save(): `try { await ref.read(userRepositoryProvider).update(uid, {'gymId': gymId}); if (mounted) context.pop(); } finally { if (mounted) setState(() => _saving = false); }` — no catch clause.

- **[MEDIUM · navigation]** The unsaved-changes discard guard on 'Datos personales' only triggers from the custom in-app back row (_onBackTap → _showDiscardDialog when _isDirty). It is NOT protected by a PopScope, so the iOS swipe-back gesture and the Android system back button bypass the guard entirely and silently discard the user's edits (name, weight, height, gender, experience, picked avatar). This is especially relevant given the active branch is fix/workout-swipe-back — the same class of bug.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the editar-personal body in a PopScope with canPop: !_isDirty and route onPopInvokedWithResult through _showDiscardDialog, so swipe-back and system-back honor the same discard confirmation as the in-app back row.
  - **Dónde:** profile_edit_personal_screen.dart: _onBackTap/_showDiscardDialog exist but the build() returns a bare Column with no PopScope wrapper. Compare profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart line 379-385, which DOES wrap its body in PopScope(canPop:false) for onboarding mode — proving the pattern is known in the codebase.

- **[MEDIUM · consistency]** Header/back affordance is inconsistent across the four sub-screens. editar-personal, gym, and rutinas use a custom GestureDetector row (back chevron + uppercase title) inside a Column with no Scaffold/AppBar. trainer-edit is the only screen using a real Scaffold + AppBar with a standard Material back arrow and a normally-cased title. Step-to-step the back target, title casing, and top-bar metaphor all change.
  - **Fix:** Standardize one header component across the journey. Either give trainer-edit the same custom back row, or migrate the three athlete screens to the same Scaffold/AppBar — pick one and apply it everywhere so the back control and title style are predictable.
  - **Dónde:** profile_edit_personal_screen.dart, profile_gym_screen.dart, profile_routines_screen.dart all build `Column(children:[Padding(...GestureDetector(onTap: pop, child: Row(Icon(TreinoIcon.back)...'EDITAR PERFIL'/'GIMNASIO'/'MIS RUTINAS'))) ...])`. profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart line 387-395 builds `Scaffold(appBar: AppBar(title: Text(title), automaticallyImplyLeading: ...))`.

- **[MEDIUM · consistency]** Save/primary-action buttons differ in shape, label, and busy indicator across steps. editar-personal uses custom pill widgets (_FilledPill/_OutlinedPill) with the busy label literally '...'. gym uses a full-width ElevatedButton (rounded-14) with an inline CircularProgressIndicator. trainer-edit uses a StadiumBorder ElevatedButton with a spinner. The disabled state and busy affordance are different on each screen.
  - **Fix:** Adopt a single shared primary-button component (with a consistent loading spinner, not the '...' string) across all edit screens. The '...' busy label in editar-personal reads as broken/placeholder versus the proper spinners elsewhere.
  - **Dónde:** editar-personal lines 500-509: `_FilledPill(label: busy ? '...' : 'GUARDAR')`. gym lines 146-176: `ElevatedButton(... child: _saving ? CircularProgressIndicator : Text('GUARDAR'))` with RoundedRectangleBorder(14). trainer-edit lines 338-365: `ElevatedButton(... shape: StadiumBorder, child: _saving ? CircularProgressIndicator : Text('GUARDAR'))`.

- **[MEDIUM · usability]** Asymmetric friction on the two destructive-adjacent SESIÓN actions, which sit next to each other in the hub. 'Cerrar sesión' fires signOut() immediately on tap with NO confirmation, while 'Eliminar cuenta' (the very next tile) is heavily guarded (bottom sheet + re-auth + loading overlay). An accidental tap on 'Cerrar sesión' logs the user straight out — and the only way back in is re-authenticating.
  - **Fix:** Add a lightweight confirm dialog before sign-out ('¿Cerrar sesión?') to match the protection level expected for a session-ending action and to reduce the friction asymmetry between the two adjacent tiles.
  - **Dónde:** profile_screen.dart lines 90-95: `ProfileSectionTile(title: 'Cerrar sesión', onTap: () => ref.read(authNotifierProvider.notifier).signOut())` — no dialog. auth_notifier.dart signOut() immediately sets AsyncLoading and calls service.signOut(). Lines 96-112: 'Eliminar cuenta' opens EliminarCuentaSheet with full confirmation.

- **[LOW · states]** The 'Mis rutinas' (rutinas) error state is a dead-end: it renders centered text 'No pudimos cargar tus rutinas. Intentá de nuevo.' but provides NO retry button. The user must back out and re-enter the screen to retry, and the copy implies an action ('Intentá de nuevo') that the UI doesn't offer.
  - **Fix:** Add a 'Reintentar' button under the error text that calls ref.invalidate(assignedRoutinesProvider(myUid)), so the copy's promise of retrying is actionable in place.
  - **Dónde:** profile_routines_screen.dart lines 62-75: `error: (_, __) => Center(child: ... Text('No pudimos cargar tus rutinas. Intentá de nuevo.'))` — no button, no ref.invalidate hook.

- **[LOW · states]** editar-personal lacks a modal/blocking loading affordance during the avatar upload + save. While saving, only the pill label changes to '...' and the buttons disable, but the form fields remain interactive-looking and there is no overlay. Avatar upload can take several seconds, so the screen looks idle/unresponsive. trainer-edit and eliminar-cuenta both use clearer spinners/overlays.
  - **Fix:** Replace the '...' label with an inline spinner inside the GUARDAR pill (matching gym/trainer-edit) and consider a subtle blocking overlay during avatar upload, so the multi-second upload step reads as in-progress rather than frozen.
  - **Dónde:** profile_edit_personal_screen.dart _save() sets _SaveState.uploading then saving, but the only UI reaction (lines 484-512) is the disabled pills with label '...'. No overlay like EliminarCuentaSheet's Positioned.fill loading layer (eliminar_cuenta_sheet.dart lines 176-206).

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** Microcopy/terminology inconsistency in the unsaved-changes flow. editar-personal labels the cancel/back action both 'DESCARTAR' (the outlined pill at the bottom) and shows a dialog whose destructive action is also 'DESCARTAR', while the safe action is 'VOLVER'. The bottom 'DESCARTAR' pill actually routes through _onBackTap (which may show the discard dialog), so the same word means both 'open the discard dialog' and 'confirm discard', which is ambiguous.
  - **Fix:** Rename the bottom outlined pill to 'CANCELAR' (intent: leave) and keep 'DESCARTAR' only for the dialog's confirm action, so the destructive verb appears once and unambiguously.
  - **Dónde:** profile_edit_personal_screen.dart line 494 `_OutlinedPill(label: 'DESCARTAR', onTap: _onBackTap)` and lines 313-324 the dialog's confirm action is also 'DESCARTAR'. _onBackTap only shows the dialog when _isDirty.

- **[LOW · microcopy-i18n]** i18n coverage is uneven across the journey, which will surface as language inconsistency once localization is enabled. The hub, cuenta section, eliminar-cuenta sheet and re-auth sheet route most strings through AppL10n, but editar-personal and trainer-edit hard-code large amounts of Spanish (field labels, validators, hints, error SnackBars) marked only with '// i18n: Fase 6 Etapa 3' TODOs. trainer-edit also hard-codes the ProfileTrainerSection subtitle ('Faltan: ...', 'Perfil completo · visible en Discovery').
  - **Fix:** Move the remaining hard-coded strings in editar-personal, trainer-edit, and ProfileTrainerSection into AppL10n so the whole journey speaks one consistently-localized voice; right now the flow is a mix of localized and literal Spanish.
  - **Dónde:** profile_edit_personal_screen.dart literals 'NOMBRE','GÉNERO','Tocá para cambiar tu foto','No pudimos guardar los cambios. Probá de nuevo.' etc. all carry only the '// i18n' comment. profile_edit_trainer_screen.dart validators 'Escribí una bio.','Mínimo \$500.' are raw strings. profile_trainer_section.dart lines 47-49 hard-code subtitle text.

## Tracking corporal y performance (Insights -> log measurement -> log performance test -> check-in)

_I traced the four steps end-to-end through the router and presentation layers. The single most important finding is that this is NOT one coherent journey for one user: the four steps are split across two personas with no UI thread connecting them. Insights (`lib/features/insights/presentation/insights_screen.dart`, route `/workout/insights`) and the check-in dialog (`lib/features/check_in/presentation/check_in_dialog.dart`, auto-shown on FeedScreen) are ATHLETE-facing. But "log measurement" (`LogMeasurementScreen`) and "log performance test" (`LogPerformanceTestScreen`) are TRAINER-only screens — both require an `athleteId`, both stamp `recordedBy = currentUidProvider` (the trainer), and both are reachable ONLY from `athlete_detail_screen.dart` (the Coach view, pushed from trainer dashboard / session & appointment sheets / trainer_coach_view). There is no athlete-facing read path at all: the only consumers of the measurement/performance providers are the trainer's `athlete_detail_screen.dart`. So an athlete can never log a measurement or see their own body/performance progress in the app — and a trainer never does the check-in or Insights flow. The journey only holds together inside the Coach module (athlete detail -> +Cargar medición -> +Cargar evaluación), and even there it is two separate full-screen forms with no guided sequence. Within each step the engineering is solid (loading/saving/error states handled, snackbars on success/failure, save button disabled while saving), but there are real friction, feedback-timing, validation, and consistency gaps detailed below. Findings cite the screen/step where each occurs._

- **[HIGH · navigation]** The four steps do not form one navigable journey. Insights and check-in are athlete-facing; 'log measurement' and 'log performance test' are trainer-only (require athleteId, stamp recordedBy = trainer uid, reachable only from the Coach athlete_detail_screen). There is no UI path that takes any single user through Insights -> log measurement -> log performance test -> check-in.
  - **Fix:** Decide and document the intended persona for this journey. If it is meant to be the athlete's own body/performance tracking, build an athlete-facing read path (e.g. an athlete 'Mi progreso' tab reusing measurementsForAthleteProvider / performanceTestsForAthleteProvider with their own uid). If it is the trainer flow, rename the journey to a Coach journey and treat Insights/check-in as separate athlete features. As-is, the journey is impossible for any one user to complete.
  - **Dónde:** LogMeasurementScreen/LogPerformanceTestScreen take `athleteId` and use `currentUidProvider` as `recordedBy` (log_measurement_screen.dart:177-181, log_performance_test_screen.dart:172-176). Both are pushed only from `athlete_detail_screen.dart` (_AntropometriaSection._openLogForm L442-449, _RendimientoSection._openLogForm L706-713), which is navigated to from trainer surfaces only (trainer_dashboard_tab, session_detail_sheet, appointment_detail_sheet, trainer_coach_view). InsightsScreen is athlete-facing (route 'insights' in router.dart:381-382, opened from Home), and CheckInDialog auto-shows on FeedScreen (feed_screen.dart:40-75).

- **[MEDIUM · navigation]** Within the only place the journey is real (Coach athlete detail), logging a measurement and logging a performance test are two disconnected full-screen forms opened from two separate '+ Cargar' links. There is no 'log measurement then continue to performance test' sequence, so a trainer doing a full assessment must find and tap two different CTAs in two different sections and dismiss two forms.
  - **Fix:** For a full evaluation session, consider an optional combined 'Nueva evaluación' entry that walks measurement -> performance in one flow, or after saving a measurement offer a 'Cargar evaluación' continuation. At minimum keep both forms but make the relationship discoverable from one place.
  - **Dónde:** _AntropometriaSection and _RendimientoSection each have their own '+ Cargar' GestureDetector opening a separate fullscreenDialog (athlete_detail_screen.dart:473-483 and 736-746). Each form pops back to athlete detail on save (log_measurement_screen.dart:208, log_performance_test_screen.dart:200) with no chaining.

- **[HIGH · usability]** Both log forms allow saving a completely empty record. No field is required and there is no validation that at least one metric was entered, so an accidental tap on GUARDAR creates an empty measurement/test that then pollutes the count and the progress chart.
  - **Fix:** Disable GUARDAR (or block _save with an inline message) until at least one numeric field is non-null. Optionally warn before saving a record with only notes.
  - **Dónde:** _save() in both screens builds the model purely from optional `_parseDouble(...)` values (all null-safe) and the save button is enabled whenever `trainerUid != null && !_saving` (log_measurement_screen.dart:231 canSave, _save L161-223; log_performance_test_screen.dart:223 canSave, _save L156-215). An all-empty form persists a record with every metric null. The count line then says e.g. '1 medición registrada' (athlete_detail_screen.dart:578) for an empty record.

- **[MEDIUM · states]** Success feedback timing is fragile: in both log forms the success SnackBar is shown AFTER Navigator.pop(), i.e. on the destination (athlete detail) ScaffoldMessenger via a context that was just popped. Depending on messenger scope this can drop the confirmation or attach it to the wrong scaffold, leaving the trainer unsure the save succeeded.
  - **Fix:** Capture the messenger before popping (`final messenger = ScaffoldMessenger.of(context);`) and call `messenger.showSnackBar(...)` after pop, or rely on the destination's own messenger. This mirrors the correct pattern already used in CheckInDialog (_SiButton captures `messenger`/`navigator` before await, check_in_dialog.dart:133-134).
  - **Dónde:** log_measurement_screen.dart:207-211 calls `Navigator.of(context).pop();` then `ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(... 'Medición guardada')` using the popped widget's context. Same pattern in log_performance_test_screen.dart:199-203 ('Evaluación guardada'). Error case is fine because it stays on the form (L212-222 / L204-214).

- **[MEDIUM · consistency]** Error-recovery behavior is inconsistent across the journey's save actions. The log forms keep the form open and let the user retry on failure (good), but every failure collapses to one generic retry string with no offline/permission-specific messaging, while check-in's failure path is the most robust and Insights' error is a dead-end.
  - **Fix:** Standardize on the check-in pattern (capture messenger/navigator, surface error, stay put, allow retry) across all three steps, and add an explicit Retry affordance to the Insights error state (currently a dead-end requiring tab/route re-entry).
  - **Dónde:** Log forms: catch(_) -> reset _saving + generic SnackBar 'No pudimos guardar...' (log_measurement_screen.dart:212-222, log_performance_test_screen.dart:204-214). Check-in: confirm() uses AsyncValue.guard and the dialog inspects `checkInNotifierProvider.hasError` to keep the dialog open and show l10n.checkInError (check_in_dialog.dart:145-149, check_in_providers.dart:36-53). Insights: error -> static 'No pudimos cargar tus insights.' with NO retry (insights_screen.dart:33-45).

- **[MEDIUM · states]** Insights error and empty states are dead-ends with no recovery action. On load error the user sees only text and must back out; the same screen renders its VOLVER button only in the data branch, so error/empty users get inconsistent navigation affordances.
  - **Fix:** Add a 'Reintentar' button to the Insights error state (invalidate weeklyInsightsProvider) and ensure a consistent way to leave the screen across loading/error/empty/data.
  - **Dónde:** insights_screen.dart error branch (L33-45) and _EmptyState (L112-144) render text only, no button; the VOLVER button (_VolverButton L528-555) is only added inside the `data` ListView (L61). The header back button exists in all states (L82-85) but there is no retry.

- **[MEDIUM · microcopy-i18n]** Inconsistent localization strategy across the journey. Check-in is fully localized via AppL10n; Insights and both log forms are hardcoded Spanish strings (including month-name arrays duplicated per file). A first-time user on a non-Spanish locale would see a mixed-language journey.
  - **Fix:** Move log-form and Insights strings into AppL10n and reuse a shared date formatter, matching the check-in step. This removes the duplicated month arrays and prevents mixed-language output.
  - **Dónde:** CheckInDialog uses AppL10n.of(context) for every string (check_in_dialog.dart:32-35,48,108,135,158). In contrast, insights_screen.dart hardcodes 'INSIGHTS', 'No pudimos cargar tus insights.', '_monthsEs' (L88,37,559-562); log_measurement_screen.dart and log_performance_test_screen.dart hardcode all labels and duplicate a `_kMonths` array (L14-28 in each) plus strings like 'Cargar medición'/'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN'.

- **[LOW · consistency]** Date/timezone display convention differs between the two log forms, a subtle inconsistency for a trainer logging both in one sitting. The performance form deliberately uses UTC to match persistence; the measurement form uses local time for its header while persisting UTC, so the two forms can show different timestamps for the same moment near midnight.
  - **Fix:** Pick one convention for both forms. The performance form already reasons that the header should match the persisted/displayed UTC value; apply the same to the measurement form to keep the two steps consistent.
  - **Dónde:** log_performance_test_screen.dart formats header with `DateTime.now().toUtc()` and documents the UTC convention (L34-41, L224-227). log_measurement_screen.dart formats header with `dt.toLocal()` (_formatDateTimeEs L30-37, `now = DateTime.now()` L232) while persisting `recordedAt: DateTime.now().toUtc()` (L181).

- **[LOW · consistency]** Primary-action button styling and labels differ across the journey's confirm actions, weakening the sense of one flow. The two log forms use a pill ElevatedButton with uppercase condensed labels ('GUARDAR MEDICIÓN' / 'GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN'); the check-in confirm uses a rounded-12 button with sentence-case l10n; Insights' only action is an outlined 'VOLVER' pill.
  - **Fix:** Align primary-button shape, casing, and label style across the flow per docs/design-system.md tokens so each step's main action reads as the same component.
  - **Dónde:** Log forms: pill (radius 9999) ElevatedButton, accent bg, uppercase 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN' (log_measurement_screen.dart:364-392) / 'GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN' (log_performance_test_screen.dart:448-476). Check-in: radius-12 ElevatedButton, l10n.checkInSiButton (check_in_dialog.dart:151-164). Insights: outlined pill 'VOLVER' (insights_screen.dart:534-552).

- **[LOW · usability]** In the performance log form, sprint sub-labels lose context after the first field. The section is 'VELOCIDAD (seg)' and the first field is 'Sprint 10m', but the rest are just '20m', '30m', '40m', so a scanning trainer or first-timer sees bare distances without the 'Sprint' qualifier.
  - **Fix:** Use consistent labels ('Sprint 20m', etc.) or a sub-group header that makes the 'Sprint' context unmistakable for every field.
  - **Dónde:** log_performance_test_screen.dart: labels 'Sprint 10m' (L319), then '20m' (L326), '30m' (L333), '40m' (L340) under section 'VELOCIDAD (seg)' (L316).

- **[LOW · usability]** The measurement form's long collapsible 'CIRCUNFERENCIAS' section (17 fields) starts collapsed and is the bulk of the form, while body-composition fields are always visible. A first-time trainer may not realize how much data the form captures, and the keyboard can obscure lower fields despite the fixed 80px spacer.
  - **Fix:** Add a brief hint of what the collapsed section contains (e.g. count or sub-group names in the subtitle) and use MediaQuery.viewInsets-aware bottom padding so focused lower fields stay visible above the keyboard.
  - **Dónde:** _CircumferencesSection defaults `_expanded = false` (log_measurement_screen.dart:600); expanding reveals TRONCO/TREN SUPERIOR/TREN INFERIOR with 17 inputs (L658-747). The form relies on a fixed `SizedBox(height: 80)` spacer (L352) rather than viewInsets-aware padding for keyboard avoidance.

- **[LOW · states]** Check-in is single-shot per process: if the athlete dismisses it (NO) or it errors and they give up, it will not reappear that session, and there is no manual way to check in later from the feed. A user who taps NO by accident has no obvious recovery within the session.
  - **Fix:** Provide a persistent manual 'Check-in' affordance on the feed (or in Mi Gym) so a user who dismissed or failed the auto-prompt can still check in during the same session.
  - **Dónde:** feed_screen.dart:_maybeShowCheckIn marks `_checkInDialogShownThisSessionProvider = true` BEFORE showing the dialog (L62) and returns early on subsequent mounts (L47); NO button just pops (check_in_dialog.dart:69-72). No alternate manual check-in entry point was found in the feed.
